# ⚙️ config.yml | CustomCrops | XiaoMoMi Plugins

Copy

    # Do not change this value
    config-version: '${config_version}'
    # Enable or disable debugging mode
    debug: false
    # Enable or disable metrics collection using BStats
    metrics: true
    # Enable automatic update checks
    update-checker: true
    # Force the locale (e.g., zh_cn)
    force-locale: ''
    # World settings
    worlds:
      # Some servers use separate directories for player worlds, which may not be in the server's root directory.
      # This option allows you to specify a custom path to these world folders. This is only applicable for Bukkit worlds.
      absolute-world-folder-path: ''
      # Specifies which worlds the plugin's mechanisms should apply to
      # Options: whitelist/blacklist/regex
      mode: blacklist
      list:
        - blacklist_world # A world that doesn't exist
      settings:
        # Default settings that apply to all worlds
        _DEFAULT_:
          # Whether to enable the plugin's pre-configured systems
          # Disabling this stops all mechanisms from ticking unless fully managed via the API.
          # If you're not familiar with using CustomCropsAPI, keep this set to true as it meets the needs of 99% of users.
          enable: true
          # Seasonal settings
          season:
            enable: true
            # Automatically cycle through seasons
            auto-alternation: true
            # Duration of each season in game days
            duration: 28
          # This is different from the vanilla RandomTickSpeed.
          # "Random tick" here means randomly selecting n blocks within a 16x16x16 section every second for ticking, unlike Minecraft's per-tick approach.
          # Therefore, CustomCrops' random ticks have minimal impact on the server and run on multiple threads.
          random-tick-speed: 20
          # The minimum tick interval in seconds when using scheduled tick mode
          # A value of 180s means a crop is guaranteed to tick at least once every 180 seconds
          # For crops, growth rates are nearly uniform under the same conditions
          # Sprinklers and pots operate periodically within this interval.
          min-tick-unit: 180
          # Settings for ticking while the world is offline
          # Allows crops to grow even if the world is unloaded or the server is down
          # This might cause issues with time-dependent conditions like seasons
          offline-tick:
            enable: false
            # Maximum offline time recorded in seconds
            # Avoid setting this too high, as it may cause long-unloaded chunks to take a long time to load
            max-offline-seconds: 1200
            # Maximum time allowed for loading a chunk
            # Sometimes, chunks with large amounts of data that have been unloaded for a long time can take a while to load,
            # potentially causing unexpected issues
            # This setting allows the plugin to forcibly interrupt the tick process if loading time exceeds a set threshold
            max-loading-time: 100 #ms
          # Crop settings
          crop:
            # [RANDOM_TICK]
            # Random tick mode mirrors vanilla behavior, where crops grow randomly
            # This randomness can cause significant stage differences among crops grown under identical conditions
            # [SCHEDULED_TICK]
            # Scheduled tick mode provides more predictable growth management,
            # ensuring crops grow at nearly the same rate
            mode: RANDOM_TICK
            # Tick interval determines how many times a block is ticked before its logic is executed
            tick-interval: 1
            # Limit the number of crops per chunk (-1 means no limit)
            max-per-chunk: -1
          # Pot settings
          pot:
            # RANDOM_TICK or SCHEDULED_TICK
            mode: SCHEDULED_TICK
            tick-interval: 3
            max-per-chunk: -1
          # Sprinkler settings
          sprinkler:
            # RANDOM_TICK or SCHEDULED_TICK
            mode: SCHEDULED_TICK
            tick-interval: 2
            max-per-chunk: -1
        # Override default settings for specific worlds here
        _WORLDS_:
          world_nether:
            enable: false
          world_the_end:
            enable: false
    # Mechanics settings
    mechanics:
      # Create additional ranks by adding more slashes, e.g., x/x/x/x/x
      # "x" represents weight, which determines the probability proportion
      # 17/2/1 = 85%/10%/5%
      # 85% is calculated as 17/(17+2+1) * 100%
      default-quality-ratio: 17/2/1
      # Scarecrow settings to prevent crops from being attacked by crows
      scarecrow:
        enable: true
        id: 'scarecrow'
        type: ITEM_FRAME
        range: 7
        # If enabled, the scarecrow's range will not be limited
        # It will protect all crops within the same chunk
        protect-chunk: false
      # Greenhouse glass prevents crops from withering due to seasonal changes
      greenhouse:
        enable: true
        # You can use a list of IDs here; vanilla blocks are also supported
        id: 'greenhouse_glass'
        type: CHORUS
        range: 5
      # Synchronize seasons with another world
      sync-season:
        enable: false
        reference: world
      # Vanilla farmland mechanics
      vanilla-farmland:
        # Disable the moisture mechanics of vanilla farmland
        # This is useful if you prefer vanilla farmland but the water system conflicts with vanilla mechanics
        disable-moisture-mechanic: false
        # Prevent entities from trampling farmland
        prevent-trampling: false
      # Set hologram offset correction for different blocks
      hologram-offset-correction:
        "crop_stage_death": 0
      # Specify block types that should be overridden by the plugin
      # Some common crops: WHEAT/CARROTS/POTATOES/BEETROOTS/SWEET_BERRY_BUSH
      override-vanilla-blocks: []
    other-settings:
      # It is recommended to use MiniMessage format. If you want to use legacy color codes ("&"), enable support below.
      # Disabling this can improve performance
      legacy-color-code-support: true
      # Requires PlaceholderAPI to function
      placeholder-register:
        '{skill-level}': '%levelplugin_farming%'
      # To use items from other plugins
      item-detection-order: []
      # Whether to protect the original lore of items
      # Uses the scoreboard component to identify the plugin's lore,
      # which may conflict with some plugins still using SpigotAPI#ItemMeta
      protect-original-lore: false
      # Whether to verify if a block/furniture matches the data in CustomCrops
      # Enable this if using Oraxen, as its API is more reliable
      double-check: false

# Custom Season Provider | CustomCrops | XiaoMoMi Plugins

Create a class that implements `SeasonProvider` and then register it on plugin enable

Copy

    package net.momirealms.customcrops.api.example;
    
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.world.Season;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.integration.SeasonProvider;
    import org.bukkit.World;
    import org.jetbrains.annotations.NotNull;
    
    public class MySeasonProvider implements SeasonProvider {
        
        @Override
        public @NotNull Season getSeason(@NotNull World world) {
            return ...;
        }
    
        @Override
        public String identifier() {
            return "MySeasonPlugin";
        }
    }

[PreviousOther Block Systemchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customcrops/plugin-wiki/customcrops/api/other-block-system)

Last updated 1 year ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    package net.momirealms.customcrops.api.example;
    
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.BukkitCustomCropsPlugin;
    import org.bukkit.plugin.java.JavaPlugin;
    
    public class MyPlugin extends JavaPlugin {
    
        @Override
        public void onEnable() {
            register();
        }
    
        public void register() {
            BukkitCustomCropsPlugin.getInstance().getIntegrationManager().registerSeasonProvider(new MySeasonProvider());
        }
    }

# ⌨️ API | CustomCrops | XiaoMoMi Plugins

Before using the CustomCrops API, make sure you have imported the Paper API.

[![Logo](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fassets.papermc.io%2Fweb%2Fandroid-chrome-512x512.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be86b5e3&sv=2)Project setup | PaperMC Docsdocs.papermc.iochevron-right](https://docs.papermc.io/paper/dev/project-setup)

Then you can add the CustomCrops API dependency to your project

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customcrops/plugin-wiki/customcrops/api#repository)

📌 Repository

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customcrops/plugin-wiki/customcrops/api#dependency)

📌 Dependency

At last, don't forget to add CustomCrops to plugin.yml

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customcrops/plugin-wiki/customcrops/api/basic-operations#get-remove-blockstate)

Get/Remove Blockstate

Copy

    CustomCropsWorld<?> world = ...;
    world.getBlockState(pos3);
    world.removeBlockState(pos3);

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customcrops/plugin-wiki/customcrops/api/basic-operations#add-blockstate)

Add Blockstate

Copy

    CropBlock cropBlock = (CropBlock) BuiltInBlockMechanics.CROP.mechanic();
    CustomCropsBlockState blockState = cropBlock.createBlockState();
    cropBlock.id(blockState, "tomato");
    cropBlock.point(blockState, 0);
    world.addBlockState(pos3, blockState);

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customcrops/plugin-wiki/customcrops/api/basic-operations#set-remove-get-custom-data-in-blockstate)

Set/Remove/Get Custom Data in Blockstate

Copy

    SynchronizedCompoundMap compoundMap = blockState.compoundMap();
    compoundMap.remove("key");
    compoundMap.put("key", new StringTag("key", "test"));
    compoundMap.get("key");

# Other Block System | CustomCrops | XiaoMoMi Plugins

In addition to the oraxen and ItemsAdder compatibility provided by the plugin, you can also adapt customcrops to your own server, especially for some large servers with independent development capabilities.

To adapt your own plugin to customcrops you only need to implement two classes: `AbstractCustomEventListener` & `CustomItemProvider`

Copy

    package net.momirealms.customcrops.api.example;
    
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.AbstractCustomEventListener;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.AbstractItemManager;
    import org.bukkit.event.EventHandler;
    
    public class MyCustomListener extends AbstractCustomEventListener {
    
        public MyCustomListener(AbstractItemManager itemManager) {
            super(itemManager);
        }
    
        @EventHandler(ignoreCancelled = true)
        public void onInteractFurniture(FurnitureInteractEvent event) {
            itemManager.handlePlayerInteractFurniture(...);
        }
    
        @EventHandler(ignoreCancelled = true)
        public void onInteractCustomBlock(CustomBlockInteractEvent event) {
            itemManager.handlePlayerInteractBlock(...);
        }
    
        @EventHandler(ignoreCancelled = true)
        public void onBreakFurniture(FurnitureBreakEvent event) {
            itemManager.handlePlayerBreak(...);
        }
    
        @EventHandler(ignoreCancelled = true)
        public void onBreakCustomBlock(CustomBlockBreakEvent event) {
            itemManager.handlePlayerBreak(..);
        }
        
        @EventHandler(ignoreCancelled = true)
        public void onPlaceFurniture(FurniturePlaceEvent event) {
            itemManager.handlePlayerPlace(...);
        }
        
        @EventHandler(ignoreCancelled = true)
        public void onPlaceCustomBlock(CustomBlockPlaceEvent event) {
            itemManager.handlePlayerPlace(...);
        }
    }

At last, register them on plugin enable

[PreviousPlugin Eventschevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customcrops/plugin-wiki/customcrops/api/plugin-events)
[NextCustom Season Providerchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customcrops/plugin-wiki/customcrops/api/custom-season-provider)

Last updated 1 year ago

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    package net.momirealms.customcrops.api.example;
    
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.CustomItemProvider;
    import org.bukkit.Location;
    import org.bukkit.block.Block;
    import org.bukkit.entity.Entity;
    import org.bukkit.entity.Player;
    import org.bukkit.inventory.ItemStack;
    import org.checkerframework.checker.nullness.qual.Nullable;
    
    public class MyCustomItemProvider implements CustomItemProvider {
    
        @Override
        public boolean removeCustomBlock(Location location) {
            return ...;
        }
    
        @Override
        public boolean placeCustomBlock(Location location, String id) {
            return ...;
        }
    
        @Override
        public @Nullable Entity placeFurniture(Location location, String id) {
            return ...;
        }
    
        @Override
        public boolean removeFurniture(Entity entity) {
            return ...;
        }
    
        @Override
        public @Nullable String blockID(Block block) {
            return ...;
        }
    
        @Override
        public @Nullable String itemID(ItemStack itemStack) {
            return ...;
        }
    
        @Override
        public @Nullable ItemStack itemStack(Player player, String id) {
            return ...;
        }
    
        @Override
        public @Nullable String furnitureID(Entity entity) {
            return ...;
        }
    
        @Override
        public boolean isFurniture(Entity entity) {
            return ...;
        }
    }

Copy

    package net.momirealms.customcrops.api.example;
    
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.BukkitCustomCropsPlugin;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.AbstractItemManager;
    import org.bukkit.plugin.java.JavaPlugin;
    
    public class MyPlugin extends JavaPlugin {
    
        @Override
        public void onEnable() {
            register();
        }
    
        public void register() {
            AbstractItemManager itemManager = BukkitCustomCropsPlugin.getInstance().getItemManager();
            MyCustomListener listener = new MyCustomListener(itemManager);
            MyCustomItemProvider provider = new MyCustomItemProvider();
            itemManager.setCustomEventListener(listener);
            itemManager.setCustomItemProvider(provider);
        }
    }

# Custom Mechanism | CustomCrops | XiaoMoMi Plugins

This page will use sugarcane as an example to roughly implement a mechanism similar to the vanilla sugarcane.

Firstly create two classes for both item and block

Copy

    package net.momirealms.customcrops.api.example;
    
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.item.AbstractCustomCropsItem;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.common.util.Key;
    
    public class SugarCaneItem extends AbstractCustomCropsItem {
        
        private static SugarCaneItem instance;
    
        public SugarCaneItem() {
            super(Key.key("customcrops", "sugarcane_item"));
        }
    
        public static SugarCaneItem instance() {
            if (instance == null) {
                instance = new SugarCaneItem();
            }
            return instance;
        }
    }

Then register it in `onEnable()` method

Then we can create some basic logics for instance placing the sugarcane block

Now you should be able to plant the sugarcane (I used a pineapple as a substitute in the gif because I haven't prepared the model for sugarcane yet)

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fi.imgur.com%2Ff3eQwD8.gif&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bcc43a75&sv=2)

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3367277500-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F3tsXOZ7EnqaBWiFptXXV%252Fuploads%252F7lsytwLmI3BujY3EkYps%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33771e2c-ebe2-4976-9454-b328816fbf0a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b1c00579&sv=2)

insight mode

Then we can configure the grow/break logics for sugarcane

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fi.imgur.com%2FYTNxP7R.gif&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=58c4cf8f&sv=2)

[PreviousBasic Operationschevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customcrops/plugin-wiki/customcrops/api/basic-operations)
[NextPlugin Eventschevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customcrops/plugin-wiki/customcrops/api/plugin-events)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    package net.momirealms.customcrops.api.example;
    
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.block.AbstractCustomCropsBlock;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.common.util.Key;
    
    public class SugarCaneBlock extends AbstractCustomCropsBlock {
    
        private static SugarCaneBlock instance;
    
        private SugarCaneBlock() {
            super(Key.key("customcrops", "sugarcane_block"));
        }
    
        // This method is used to verify whether a block belongs to this mechanism
        // The id would be the item ID from the custom item plugin for instance Oraxen
        @Override
        public boolean isBlockInstance(String id) {
            return id.equals("customcrops:sugarcane_block_id");
        }
        
        public static SugarCaneBlock instance() {
            if (instance == null) {
                instance = new SugarCaneBlock();
            }
            return instance;
        }
        
        @Override
        public NamedTextColor insightColor() {
            return NamedTextColor.YELLOW;
        }
    }

Copy

    package net.momirealms.customcrops.api.example;
    
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.BukkitCustomCropsPlugin;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.Registries;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.RegistryAccess;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.event.CustomCropsReloadEvent;
    import org.bukkit.event.EventHandler;
    import org.bukkit.event.Listener;
    import org.bukkit.plugin.java.JavaPlugin;
    
    import java.util.List;
    
    public class YourPlugin extends JavaPlugin implements Listener {
    
        @Override
        public void onEnable() {
            RegistryAccess access = BukkitCustomCropsPlugin.getInstance().getRegistryAccess();
            access.registerBlockMechanic(SugarCaneBlock.instance());
            access.registerItemMechanic(SugarCaneItem.instance());
            getServer().getPluginManager().registerEvents(this, this);
        }
    
        @EventHandler
        public void onPluginReload(CustomCropsReloadEvent event) {
            // ITEMS and BLOCKS are temporary mappings to associate item id with mechanism type
            // For example, if you have multiple blocks with the same mechanism, such as red wool, green wool, and gray wool, you need to register them in this registry.
            // This registry is cleared when the plugin is reloaded to apply changes to the configuration file
            // NOTE: NEVER USE THE REGISTRIES ANNOTATED WITH @DONOTUSE
            for (String sugarcaneItem : List.of("customcrops:sugarcane_item_id")) {
                Registries.ITEMS.register(sugarcaneItem, SugarCaneItem.instance());
            }
            for (String sugarcaneBlock : List.of("customcrops:sugarcane_block_id")) {
                Registries.BLOCKS.register(sugarcaneBlock, SugarCaneBlock.instance());
            }
        }
    }

Copy

    package net.momirealms.customcrops.api.example;
    
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.BukkitCustomCropsPlugin;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.ExistenceForm;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.InteractionResult;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.item.AbstractCustomCropsItem;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.world.CustomCropsBlockState;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.world.CustomCropsWorld;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.world.Pos3;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.wrapper.WrappedInteractEvent;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.util.LocationUtils;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.common.util.Key;
    import org.bukkit.Location;
    import org.bukkit.Material;
    import org.bukkit.block.Block;
    import org.bukkit.block.BlockFace;
    import org.bukkit.entity.Entity;
    import org.bukkit.entity.Item;
    import org.bukkit.entity.Player;
    
    import java.util.Collection;
    import java.util.List;
    
    public class SugarCaneItem extends AbstractCustomCropsItem {
    
        private static SugarCaneItem instance;
    
        public SugarCaneItem() {
            super(Key.key("customcrops", "sugarcane_item"));
        }
    
        public static SugarCaneItem instance() {
            if (instance == null) {
                instance = new SugarCaneItem();
            }
            return instance;
        }
    
        @Override
        public InteractionResult interactAt(WrappedInteractEvent wrapped) {
            // Sugarcane should be planted on blocks
            if (wrapped.existenceForm() != ExistenceForm.BLOCK)
                return InteractionResult.PASS;
            // Sugarcane should be planted on the upper face
            if (wrapped.clickedBlockFace() != BlockFace.UP)
                return InteractionResult.PASS;
            // Get the location of the clicked block
            Location location = wrapped.location();
    
            Block block = location.getBlock();
            // should be planted on sand or dirt
            if (block.getType() != Material.SAND && block.getType() != Material.RED_SAND && block.getType() != Material.DIRT) {
                return InteractionResult.PASS;
            }
    
            // should be planted near water
            outer: {
                for (BlockFace face : List.of(BlockFace.NORTH, BlockFace.SOUTH, BlockFace.EAST, BlockFace.WEST)) {
                    if (block.getRelative(face).getType() == Material.WATER) {
                        break outer;
                    }
                }
                return InteractionResult.PASS;
            }
    
            // check if the place is suitable for planting
            Location sugarcaneLocation = location.clone().add(0,1,0);
            if (!suitableForPlant(sugarcaneLocation)) {
                return InteractionResult.PASS;
            }
    
            // reduce the amount of item
            wrapped.itemInHand().setAmount(wrapped.itemInHand().getAmount() - 1);
    
    
            // Get the CustomCrops world and add block state
            CustomCropsWorld<?> world = wrapped.world();
            CustomCropsBlockState newBlockState = SugarCaneBlock.instance().createBlockState();
            world.addBlockState(Pos3.from(sugarcaneLocation), newBlockState);
    
            // place the block
            BukkitCustomCropsPlugin.getInstance().getItemManager().placeBlock(sugarcaneLocation, "customcrops:sugarcane_block_id");
    
            return InteractionResult.COMPLETE;
        }
    
        private boolean suitableForPlant(Location location) {
            Block block = location.getBlock();
            if (block.getType() != Material.AIR) return false;
            Location center = LocationUtils.toBlockCenterLocation(location);
            Collection<Entity> entities = center.getWorld().getNearbyEntities(center, 0.5,0.5,0.5);
            entities.removeIf(entity -> (entity instanceof Player || entity instanceof Item));
            return entities.isEmpty();
        }
    }

Copy

    package net.momirealms.customcrops.api.example;
    
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.BukkitCustomCropsPlugin;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.block.AbstractCustomCropsBlock;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.world.CustomCropsBlockState;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.world.CustomCropsWorld;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.world.Pos3;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.core.wrapper.WrappedBreakEvent;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.misc.NamedTextColor;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.api.util.LocationUtils;
    import net.momirealms.customcrops.common.util.Key;
    import org.bukkit.Location;
    import org.bukkit.Material;
    import org.bukkit.block.Block;
    import org.bukkit.entity.Entity;
    import org.bukkit.entity.Item;
    import org.bukkit.entity.Player;
    import org.bukkit.inventory.ItemStack;
    
    import java.util.Collection;
    import java.util.Optional;
    
    public class SugarCaneBlock extends AbstractCustomCropsBlock {
    
        private static SugarCaneBlock instance;
    
        private SugarCaneBlock() {
            super(Key.key("customcrops", "sugarcane_block"));
        }
    
        @Override
        public boolean isBlockInstance(String id) {
            return id.equals("customcrops:sugarcane_block_id");
        }
    
        public static SugarCaneBlock instance() {
            if (instance == null) {
                instance = new SugarCaneBlock();
            }
            return instance;
        }
    
        @Override
        public void randomTick(CustomCropsBlockState state, CustomCropsWorld<?> world, Pos3 location, boolean offlineTick) {
            // firstly check if it's the top block
            Pos3 upper = location.add(0,1,0);
            Optional<CustomCropsBlockState> upperState = world.getBlockState(upper);
            if (upperState.isPresent() && upperState.get().type() instanceof SugarCaneBlock) {
                return;
            }
    
            // get the current height
            int height = 1;
            for (int i = 1; i < 4; i++) {
                Pos3 under = location.add(0,-i,0);
                Optional<CustomCropsBlockState> optionalState = world.getBlockState(under);
                if (optionalState.isPresent() && optionalState.get().type() instanceof SugarCaneBlock) {
                    height++;
                } else {
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (height >= 4) return;
    
            // check if there's enough space for growing
            Location upperBukkitLocation = upper.toLocation(world.bukkitWorld());
            // switch to the main thread
            BukkitCustomCropsPlugin.getInstance().getScheduler().sync().run(() -> {
                if (!suitableForGrow(upperBukkitLocation)) {
                    return;
                }
                // place the upper block
                BukkitCustomCropsPlugin.getInstance().getItemManager().placeBlock(upperBukkitLocation, "customcrops:sugarcane_block_id");
                world.addBlockState(upper, createBlockState());
            }, upperBukkitLocation);
        }
    
        private boolean suitableForGrow(Location location) {
            Block block = location.getBlock();
            if (block.getType() != Material.AIR) return false;
            Location center = LocationUtils.toBlockCenterLocation(location);
            Collection<Entity> entities = center.getWorld().getNearbyEntities(center, 0.5,0.5,0.5);
            entities.removeIf(entity -> (entity instanceof Player || entity instanceof Item));
            return entities.isEmpty();
        }
    
        @Override
        public void onBreak(WrappedBreakEvent event) {
            Location location = event.location();
            Pos3 pos3 = Pos3.from(location);
            CustomCropsWorld<?> world = event.world();
    
            // build the item
            ItemStack itemToDrop = BukkitCustomCropsPlugin.getInstance().getItemManager().build(null, "customcrops:sugarcane_item_id");
    
            // break the upper blocks
            for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
                Pos3 upper = pos3.add(0, i,0);
                Optional<CustomCropsBlockState> optionalState = world.getBlockState(upper);
                if (optionalState.isPresent() && optionalState.get().type() instanceof SugarCaneBlock) {
                    world.removeBlockState(upper);
                    Location temp = upper.toLocation(world.bukkitWorld());
                    BukkitCustomCropsPlugin.getInstance().getItemManager().removeBlock(temp);
                    temp.getWorld().dropItemNaturally(temp, itemToDrop);
                } else {
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    
        @Override
        public NamedTextColor insightColor() {
            return NamedTextColor.YELLOW;
        }
    }

# bossbar.yml | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

**Bossbar Section:** You can create multiple bossbar sections, each with its own settings. In this example, we have a `bossbar_1` section. But you can create more for instance `bossbar_2`

Copy

    # You can create as many bossbar sections as you'd like
    bossbar_1: ...
    
    bossbar_2: ...

**Bossbar Color:** Choose the color of the bossbar using the `color` field. The available options are: `BLUE`, `GREEN`, `PINK`, `PURPLE`, `RED`, `WHITE`, and `YELLOW`. For this example, the color is set to `YELLOW`.

If you need to hide a specific bossbar, you need to modify the configuration in config.yml

Copy

    bossbar_1:
      # BLUE, GREEN, PINK, PURPLE, RED, WHITE, YELLOW
      color: YELLOW

**Progress Bar Style:** Set the appearance of the progress bar with the `overlay` field. Options include `"progress"`, `"notched_6"`, `"notched_10"`, `"notched_12"`, and `"notched_20"`. Here, it is set to `PROGRESS`.

Copy

    bossbar_1:
      # "progress", "notched_6", "notched_10", "notched_12", "notched_20"
      overlay: PROGRESS

**Conditions:** You can define conditions that must be met for the bossbar to be displayed. In the `conditions` section, each condition has a type (e.g., `permission`) and a `refresh-interval` to prevent heavy conditions from lagging the server. The `value` field lists the permissions required. For example, if a player has the `bossbar.show` permission, the bossbar will be shown.

You can view all supported conditions here [✅ Condition](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/condition)

Copy

    bossbar_1:
      conditions:
        condition_1:
          type: permission
          refresh-interval: 20  # How often, in ticks, to check if the player still has the required permission
          value:
            - bossbar.show

**Text Display Order:** The bossbar can display a sequence of messages, defined under `text-display-order`. Each message has a `duration` (in ticks, where 20 ticks = 1 second) and the text to display. For example:

*   The first message (`text: '%np_background_hello%'`) displays for 100 ticks (5 seconds).
    
*   The second message (`text: '%np_background_time% %np_background_location% %np_background_weather%'`) displays for 200 ticks (10 seconds).
    
*   The third message (`text: '%np_background_update%'`) displays for 100 ticks (5 seconds).
    

You can add conditions for specific text messages. In the third message, a condition is defined that checks if the player has the `nameplates.admin` permission and if the value `%np_is-latest%` equals `false`. Only if both conditions are met will this message be displayed.

If you don't need the text of the carousel, just configure it like this

[Previousconfig.ymlchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/config.yml)
[Nextactionbar.ymlchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/actionbar.yml)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    bossbar_1:
      # The bossbar will cycle through the text in this exact order:
      text-display-order:
        1:
          duration: 100
          text: '%np_background_hello%'
        2:
          duration: 200
          text: '%np_background_time%  %np_background_location%  %np_background_weather%'
          refresh-frequency: 1
        3:
          duration: 100
          text: '%np_background_update%'
          conditions:
            permission: nameplates.admin
            equals:
              value1: '%np_is-latest%'
              value2: 'false'

Copy

    bossbar_1:
      text: '%np_background_hello%'

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# actionbar.yml | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

**Conditions:** You can define specific conditions under which the actionbar will be shown. In this case, the `condition_1` checks whether a player has the `actionbar.show` permission. The `refresh-interval` specifies how often, in ticks, the permission should be rechecked (20 ticks = 1 second). The permission check ensures only players with the proper permission will see the actionbar.

You can view all supported conditions here [✅ Condition](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/condition)

Copy

    actionbar:
      conditions:
        condition_1:
          type: permission
          refresh-interval: 20  # Refresh rate, in ticks, to recheck the permission status
          value:
            - actionbar.show

**Text Display Order:** This section determines the order in which the actionbar messages are displayed. Each message has a:

*   **Duration:** The time the text will be visible, measured in ticks. For example, `duration: -1` means the message will stay on the screen indefinitely until manually removed or replaced.
    
*   **Text:** This defines the message that will appear in the actionbar. For example, `%np_conditional_actionbar%` is the placeholder text being displayed.
    

Copy

    actionbar:
      text-display-order:
        1:
          duration: -1
          text: '%np_conditional_actionbar%'
          conditions: {}

In the case of only one carousel text, this configuration is equivalent

[Previousbossbar.ymlchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/bossbar.yml)
[Nextbubble.ymlchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/bubble.yml)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    actionbar:
      text: '%np_conditional_actionbar%'

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# advance-data.yml | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/advance-data.yml#default-advance)

**Default Advance:**

The `default` value defines the default width (in pixels or another unit) for characters in a font. In this file, all the entries have a `default` value of `9.0`, meaning those unknown characters will have a width of 9 units unless specified otherwise in the `values` section.

Copy

    # namespace:font
    minecraft:default:
      # default advance
      default: 9.0

**Template Loading Sequence:** This specifies the order in which font templates (character sets) will be loaded. The sequence includes:

*   `unifont` (a Unicode font),
    
*   `nonlatin_european` (for non-Latin European characters),
    
*   `accented` (accented characters),
    
*   `ascii` (standard ASCII characters),
    
*   `space` (handling spaces).
    

Copy

    minecraft:default:
      template-loading-sequence: # templates are registered in config.yml
        - unifont
        - nonlatin_european
        - accented
        - ascii
        - space

**Override Values:** Specific characters can have their widths overridden in the `values` section. For example, the character `默` has a width of `9.0`.

[Previousnameplate.ymlchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/nameplate.yml)
[Next➕️ Add New Contentschevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/add-new-contents)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    minecraft:default:
      values:
        默: 9.0

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# 🖼️ Background | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

Basics

Background is made up of three parts: left middle and right. I think it's easy to understand how the background works. The plugin obtains the width of your text and uses the binary search method to piece together a background image that adapts to the text.

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/add-new-contents/background#add-a-new-background-configuration)

Add a new background configuration


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FIdlam4Pz8QEWhTdXXRhV%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b352e90&sv=2)

Background config contains 9 images and a YAML config file.

**height/ascent**:

> *   height: The height of the character, measured in pixels. Can be negative. This tag is separate from the area used in the source texture and just rescales the displayed result.
>     
> *   ascent: The ascent of the character, measured in pixels. This value adds a vertical shift to the displayed result.
>     

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2Fa6RV4rgppGGc12PGgz2O%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3c1c4b&sv=2)

[Next💬 Bubblechevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/add-new-contents/bubble)

    left:
      image: b0
      height: 14
      ascent: 7
    
    right:
      image: b0
      height: 14
      ascent: 7
    
    middle:
      height: 14
      ascent: 7

# Static Text | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

**Static-text** will always occupy a fixed text width, meaning the width of the text and the generated offset characters will be constant. This ensures that the layout remains consistent, regardless of the actual content, which is useful for maintaining uniform spacing in the display.

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FGy2sr5UHcgTkCkXGbQ0w%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95c0f4e9&sv=2)

Copy

    static-text:
      money_hud:
        position: right  # right / middle / left
        text: '%np_image_coin% %np_shift_money%'
        value: 180

For example, if your text width is 50px, the plugin will generate a transparent image with a total width of 130px. This results in a combined width of 180px (50 + 130 = 180).

[PreviousConditional Textchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/conditional-text)
[NextVanilla Hudchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/vanilla-hud)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Switch Text | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

The `switch-text` feature maps the result of a variable (such as the player's world name) to other values based on the content of the `switch` option. The `default` setting determines what text should be displayed if no matching value is found in the mapping. This allows for flexible text customization based on different variable conditions, ensuring that appropriate text is shown even when a match isn't available.

Copy

    switch-text:
      world:
        switch: '%player_world%'
        case:
          'world': "<green>Overworld</green>"
          'world_nether': "<red>The Nether</red>"
          'world_the_end': "<red>The End</red>"
        default: "<gray>Unknown world</gray>"

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2Fwv7sz7ua0V0W7NnDkqtZ%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd63f5fe&sv=2)

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FmmiPEdZGJO85YEtlMKTB%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2253fc5b&sv=2)

[Previous🅿️ Custom Placeholderschevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders)
[NextBackground/Nameplate/Bubble Textchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/background-nameplate-bubble-text)

# 🔶 Image | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

You can create as many images as you want in CustomNameplates

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FhfDUUFC9v5lxLkRWwxPl%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21ab4a04&sv=2)

    image: bell
    height: 10
    ascent: 4

**height/ascent**:

> *   height: The height of the character, measured in pixels. Can be negative. This tag is separate from the area used in the source texture and just rescales the displayed result.
>     
> *   ascent: The ascent of the character, measured in pixels. This value adds a vertical shift to the displayed result.
>     

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/add-new-contents/image#how-to-create-images-without-shadow)

How to create images without Shadow?

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/add-new-contents/image#for-1.21.4)

For 1.21.4+

[![Logo](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fassets.papermc.io%2Fweb%2Fandroid-chrome-512x512.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be86b5e3&sv=2)Format | PaperMC Docsdocs.advntr.devchevron-right](https://docs.advntr.dev/minimessage/format.html#shadow-color)

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/add-new-contents/image#for-1.21.3-and-below)

For 1.21.3 and below

To create images without shadow you should set the image's **alpha** to 254 (In another way, it's the transparency). For the moment you can only do that with an image editor for instance Aseprite/PhotoShop.

Or you can just configure like this, the plugin would process the image for you

If you still don't know how to do that, plugin provides another way to remove shadow easily where you can surround your images with tag.

[Next🅿️ Custom Placeholderschevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders)

Last updated 1 year ago

Copy

    image: bell
    height: 10
    ascent: 4
    shadow: false

Copy

    <#FFFEFD>IMAGE</#FFFEFD>  # legacy method
    <#F0F0F0>IMAGE</#F0F0F0>  # new method

# Vanilla Hud | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

**Vanilla-hud** offers a HUD similar to the default health bar in Minecraft. To make it work, you simply need to provide the current value and the maximum value for the variable. The `reverse` option determines the display direction of the vanilla HUD, allowing you to control whether the bar fills from left to right or right to left. This gives flexibility in customizing how the HUD is presented in your plugin.

Copy

    vanilla-hud:
      stamina_hud:
        reverse: true
        images:
          empty: stamina_0
          half: stamina_1
          full: stamina_2
        placeholder:
          value: '1.1'
          max-value: '2'

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FeHbYYesQUzik8pyewDWQ%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=26e37e4a&sv=2)

[PreviousStatic Textchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/static-text)
[Next🅿️ Placeholderschevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/placeholders)

# nameplate.yml | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/nameplate.yml#preview-duration)

**Preview Duration:**

*   The `preview-duration` determines how long, in seconds, the nameplate preview will be shown to the player. In this configuration, it is set to 5 seconds.
    

Copy

    preview-duration: 5

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/nameplate.yml#default-nameplate)

**Default Nameplate:**

*   The `default-nameplate` defines the nameplate that will be displayed if a player's nameplate is set to "none." In this case, it is set to `'none'`, meaning no specific nameplate will be displayed by default.
    

Copy

    default-nameplate: 'none'

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/nameplate.yml#always-show-nameplate)

**Always Show Nameplate:**

*   The `always-show` option controls whether the nameplate is always visible to the player, regardless of their current state. Setting this to `false` means the nameplate will not always be visible.
    

Copy

    always-show: false

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/nameplate.yml#nameplate-configuration)

**Nameplate Configuration:**

*   **Prefix:** The `prefix` specifies a string to be displayed before the player's name. Here, `%np_switch_nameplate_color_prefix%` is used as the placeholder for colors.
    
*   **Player Name:** The `player-name` defines how the player's name is displayed. The placeholder `%np_shift_player_name%` is used here to ensure the player name remains unaffected by the client-side `Force Unicode Font` setting.
    
*   **Suffix:** The `suffix` adds a string after the player's name, here set to `%np_switch_nameplate_color_suffix%` to close color tags
    

Copy

    nameplate:
      prefix: '%np_switch_nameplate_color_prefix%'
      player-name: '%np_shift_player_name%'
      suffix: '%np_switch_nameplate_color_suffix%'

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/nameplate.yml#unlimited-tags)

**Unlimited Tags:**

The `unlimited` section defines custom tags that can be displayed along with the player's nameplate. Each tag has specific behavior and appearance settings:

*   **Tag 1:**
    
    *   **Text:** The text to be displayed, here using the placeholder `%np_tag-image%`.
        
    *   **Translation:** The `translation` field moves the tag relative to the player's nameplate, with `0,0.2,0` as the offset (X, Y, Z).
        
    *   **Viewer and Owner Conditions:** These conditions determine who can see the tag and under what circumstances. For tag\_1, the owner must:
        
        *   Have a nameplate (`has-nameplate: true`),
            
        *   Be affected by the `INVISIBILITY<0` potion effect,
            
        *   Not be disguised (`self-disguised: false`) \[Requires LibsDisguise\].
            
        
    *   **Other Attributes:** The tag is affected by crouching, the player's scale attribute, and spectator mode. It has a `line-width` of 1024 and a transparent background (`0,0,0,0`).
        
    
*   **Tag 2:** Similar to tag\_1, but with a slight adjustment in the translation (`0.01,0.2,0.01`).
    
*   **Tag 3:** This tag differs from the others in that it is only displayed when the player does **not** have a nameplate (`has-nameplate: false`). It also has a different background color (`64,0,0,0`), giving it a partially opaque black background.
    

[Previousbubble.ymlchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/bubble.yml)
[Nextadvance-data.ymlchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/advance-data.yml)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    unlimited:
      tag_1:
        text: '%np_tag-image%'
        translation: 0,0.2,0
        viewer-conditions: { }
        owner-conditions:
          has-nameplate: true
          potion-effect: "INVISIBILITY<0"
          self-disguised: false
        affected-by-crouching: true
        affected-by-scale-attribute: true
        affected-by-spectator: true
        line-width: 1024
        background-color: 0,0,0,0
      tag_2:
        text: '%np_tag-text%'
        translation: 0.01,0.2,0.01
        viewer-conditions: { }
        owner-conditions:
          has-nameplate: true
          potion-effect: "INVISIBILITY<0"
          self-disguised: false
        affected-by-crouching: true
        affected-by-scale-attribute: true
        affected-by-spectator: true
        line-width: 1024
        background-color: 0,0,0,0
      tag_3:
        text: '%np_tag-text%'
        translation: 0,0.2,0
        viewer-conditions: { }
        owner-conditions:
          has-nameplate: false
          potion-effect: "INVISIBILITY<0"
          self-disguised: false
        affected-by-crouching: true
        affected-by-scale-attribute: true
        affected-by-spectator: true
        line-width: 1024
        background-color: 64,0,0,0
        
        # other properties
        has-shadow: true
        shadow-strength: 1.0
        shadow-radius: 0.0
        is-see-through: false
        opacity: -1
        use-default-background-color: false
        alignment: CENTER
        scale: 1,1,1
        view-range: 1.0

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# 🏷️ Nameplate | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/add-new-contents/nameplate#basics)

Basics


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Nameplate is made up of three parts: left middle and right. The left and right parts will be distributed on both sides of the player name, while the middle part will copy itself to fit the length of the player name.

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/add-new-contents/nameplate#add-a-new-nameplate-configuration)

Add a new nameplate configuration


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2Fo0ygubKCHAf2wteQL5d0%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc7ccfe5&sv=2)

Nameplate config contains 3 images and a YAML config file.

Copy

    display-name: Sad Cat
    command-suggestion: Sad Cat
    min-width: 0 # This option decides the minimum width of the nameplate
    left:
      image: cat_left
      height: 16
      ascent: 12
    middle:
      image: cat_middle
      height: 16
      ascent: 12
    right:
      image: cat_right
      height: 16
      ascent: 12

**display-name**: The nameplate's display name

**height/ascent**:

> *   height: The height of the character, measured in pixels. Can be negative. This tag is separate from the area used in the source texture and just rescales the displayed result.
>     
> *   ascent: The ascent of the character, measured in pixels. This value adds a vertical shift to the displayed result.
>     

Note: In default config, most nameplate images are square, but it's not a must

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FBkgUvnda1iAkckjsG7jV%2FTG%24G1XY6HQ%28IE4%257B_%5DM5%404BP.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=992c30ed&sv=2)![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2F5AqnGzaZeqhZQl1rcxrq%2F%254VYF9JM%28R%7E5QF7ED6%25V5UH.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7bde17e9&sv=2)

[Next🖼️ Backgroundchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/add-new-contents/background)

# Conditional Text | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

**conditional-text** contains conditions and their corresponding display content. The evaluation follows a top-to-bottom order, and it is determined solely by the sequence in the configuration file, not by any `priority` settings or names. This means the first matching condition in the file is the one that will be used.

Copy

    conditional-text:
      weather:
        priority_1:
          text: 'Sunny'
          conditions:
            weather:
              - clear
        priority_2:
          text: 'Rainy'
          conditions:
            weather:
              - rain
        priority_3:
          text: 'Thunder'
          conditions:
            weather:
              - thunder

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2Fqic29ei2Ca4jBOqgOIqv%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94b2309e&sv=2)

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FDRNuLPEHLEwher5Gytr0%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=afceeff4&sv=2)

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FSGIKgV8QHoG3KcwQJiEX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=57f4791f&sv=2)

[PreviousShift Textchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/shift-text)
[NextStatic Textchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/static-text)

# 📖 Basic Font Knowledge | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/basic-font-knowledge#try-sending-texts-with-font)

Try sending texts with font

Minecraft chat component contains many decorators, one of them is font. Most of the characters are stored in `minecraft:default` font. Thin font characters are stored in `minecraft:uniform` font and enchantment table characters are stored in `minecraft:alt` font.

You can send text with font by running a simple command. It's easy to find that the same text in different fonts has different shapes.

Copy

    /tellraw @p {"text":"Hello!","font":"minecraft:default"}

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2F45fNDDWbfAZBwVTfopKh%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd06aeea&sv=2)

Copy

    /tellraw @p {"text":"Hello","font":"minecraft:uniform"}

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FQHkTugttFgdkM0BfkyVO%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5648a58&sv=2)

Copy

    /tellraw @p {"text":"Hello","font":"minecraft:alt"}

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FvJx0HV2mwAXIv8IW3NSj%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f13b5884&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/basic-font-knowledge#what-does-minecrarft-wiki-say-about-bitmap-provider)

**What does Minecrarft wiki say about "**Bitmap provider**"**

> #### 
> 
> [hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/basic-font-knowledge#bitmap-provider)
> 
> Bitmap provider
> 
> The `bitmap` provider defines simple bitmap glyphs – glyphs from textures. It references a single PNG file, a list of the characters it applies to, an optional height, and an ascent.
> 
> Textures may be any size, and glyphs may be any color. White glyphs can be colored any other color in-game. Other colors retain that tint when re-colored. Black glyphs always appear black. The glyph's widths are automatically determined based on the last right-most column of pixels containing any alpha value above 0. Glyphs themselves must not be larger than 512×512 pixels. The chars field is a list of strings. The characters inside each string entry inside this list are mapped to the corresponding positions in the referenced file. The texture is divided evenly according to the number of strings in the list, and the length of the longest string in that list.
> 
> The height field is the scale of the resulting glyph. This scale should generally match the a glyph's individual height, or be a power of it. While heights outside of this recommended range are allowed and are valid, the resulting glyphs declared inside the provider appears warped when rendered in-game. The height field is optional. When not defined, it defaults to 8, regardless of the underlying texture resolution.
> 
> The ascent field is the amount of vertical shifting is applied to the glyph. In typography, the ascent is the distance above the baseline to the cap height (top of glyph). The baseline in a glyph is the line where the descender begins. For example, in the lowercase letter y, the bottom end of the y extends past the baseline. In Vanilla, when the height is 8, the ascent is most often 7, as the descender is 1.

**In CustomNameplates you can easily understand it as**

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/basic-font-knowledge#what-are-the-benefits-of-using-other-fonts-compared-to-minecraft-default)

What are the benefits of using other fonts compared to minecraft:default?

As we can easily see that ItemsAdder and Oraxen are both using that font to register custom images. The issue is that "minecraft:default" font is the default font, so players can send the images if they found the original character. So those plugins will try their best to prevent players from sending these characters. If you don't register images into minecraft:default font, You don’t have to worry about players sending your custom images.

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/basic-font-knowledge#how-can-i-use-customnameplates-placeholders-in-other-plugin)

How can I use CustomNameplates placeholders in other plugin

Not all the plugins on the market support custom font. If you saw a plugin that supports "MiniMessage" and "PlaceholderAPI", there's 90% chance of supporting it. It's a shame that some plugin developers would convert MiniMessage into legacy format and let Spigot handle the legacy color codes.

[Previous❓️ Common Questionschevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions)
[Next⚙️ Configchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config)

*   [Try sending texts with font](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/basic-font-knowledge#try-sending-texts-with-font)
    
*   [What does Minecrarft wiki say about "Bitmap provider"](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/basic-font-knowledge#what-does-minecrarft-wiki-say-about-bitmap-provider)
    
*   [What are the benefits of using other fonts compared to minecraft:default?](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/basic-font-knowledge#what-are-the-benefits-of-using-other-fonts-compared-to-minecraft-default)
    
*   [How can I use CustomNameplates placeholders in other plugin](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/basic-font-knowledge#how-can-i-use-customnameplates-placeholders-in-other-plugin)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    image: bell # The file name
    height: 10  # The size of the image
    ascent: 4   # The Y position of the character (no higher than height)

# bubble.yml | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/bubble.yml#sender-and-viewer-requirements)

**Sender and Viewer Requirements:**

*   **Sender Requirements:** To send a bubble, the player must meet the conditions defined under `sender-requirements`. In this case:
    
    *   The player needs the `bubbles.send` permission.
        
    *   The player must also have the specified `potion-effect`, in this case, `"INVISIBILITY<0"`, which means the player doesn't have invisibility potion effect
        
    
*   **Viewer Requirements:** To view a bubble, the player must have the `bubbles.see` permission as defined under `viewer-requirements`.
    

Copy

    sender-requirements:
      permission: bubbles.send
      potion-effect: "INVISIBILITY<0"
    
    viewer-requirements:
      permission: bubbles.see

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/bubble.yml#blacklist-channels)

**Blacklist Channels:**

*   The `blacklist-channels` section allows you to specify which channels will not display bubbles. In this example:
    
    *   The channels "Private" and "Staff" are blacklisted, meaning bubbles won't be shown in these channels.
        
    
    Copy
    
        blacklist-channels:
          - Private
          - Staff
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/bubble.yml#channel-mode)

**Channel Mode:**

*   The `channel-mode` option controls who can see bubbles within channels:
    
    *   **ALL:** All players will be able to see the bubble.
        
    *   **JOINED:** Only players in the same channel can see each other's bubbles.
        
    *   **CAN\_JOIN:** Players who have permission to join specific channels will see the bubble in those channels. In this configuration, `channel-mode` is set to `ALL`, meaning all players can see the bubble.
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/bubble.yml#default-bubble)

**Default Bubble:**

*   If a player has no specific bubble assigned, the `default-bubble` setting defines which bubble should be displayed. Here, it is set to `'chat'`.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/bubble.yml#display-settings)

**Display Settings:**

*   **Y-Offset:** The `y-offset` adjusts the position of the bubble relative to the highest nameplate. In this case, it is set to `0.1`, meaning it will be displayed slightly above the nameplate.
    
*   **View Range:** The `view-range` defines how far away a player can be to still see the bubble. Here, it is set to `0.5`. (0.5 \* view distance)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/bubble.yml#bubble-display-timing)

**Bubble Display Timing:**

*   **Stay Duration:** The `stay-duration` specifies how long (in ticks) the bubble will stay visible. In this case, it is set to `150 ticks`, which equals 7.5 seconds.
    
*   **Appear and Disappear Durations:** The `appear-duration` and `disappear-duration` control how long it takes for the bubble to fade in and out. Here, the bubble will take 4 ticks (0.2 seconds) to appear and 2 ticks (0.1 seconds) to disappear.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/bubble.yml#bubble-settings)

**Bubble Settings:**

*   Under `bubble-settings`, you can configure individual bubbles:
    
    *   **Display Name:** The `display-name` is the name of the bubble; in this case, it is called `"White Bubbles"`.
        
    *   **Max Lines:** The `max-lines` setting determines how many lines of text can be displayed. For the "chat" bubble, up to 3 lines are allowed.
        
    *   **Lines:** Each line corresponds to a specific chat bubble (e.g., `chat_1`, `chat_2`, `chat_3`).
        
    *   **Line Width:** The `line-width` defines the maximum width of each line, here set to `150`.
        
    *   **Background Color:** The `background-color` specifies the ARGB values (alpha, red, green, blue) for the bubble's background. In this case, it's set to `0,0,0,0` (fully transparent).
        
    *   **Text Prefix and Suffix:** These fields allow you to add formatting to the text. The `text-prefix` here uses a `<black>` color tag and a custom font called "nameplates" with a shift effect (`shift_0`). The `text-suffix` closes the font and color tag.
        
    

[Previousactionbar.ymlchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/actionbar.yml)
[Nextnameplate.ymlchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/nameplate.yml)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    channel-mode: ALL

Copy

    default-bubble: 'chat'

Copy

    y-offset: 0.1
    view-range: 0.5

Copy

    stay-duration: 150
    appear-duration: 4
    disappear-duration: 2

Copy

    bubble-settings:
      chat:
        display-name: "White Bubbles"
        max-lines: 3
        lines:
          1: chat_1
          2: chat_2
          3: chat_3
        line-width: 150
        background-color: 0,0,0,0
        text-prefix: "<black><font:nameplates:shift_0>"
        text-suffix: "</font></black>"

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# One Time Bedrock ActionBar | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

Some users may not need to display the gold amount and simply want a black background box with the default fading effect. In that case, the following configuration can be used:

Copy

    # config.yml
    other-actionbar-stay-time: 100

Copy

    # configs/actionbar.yml
    actionbar:
      conditions:
        "!equals":
          value1: '%np_actionbar%'
          value2: ''
      text: "%np_background_other_actionbar%"

# config.yml | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/config.yml#module-settings)

**Module Settings:**

*   This section controls which modules are active:
    
    *   `nameplates`, `backgrounds`, `bubbles`, `bossbars`, `actionbars`, and `images` are all set to `true`, meaning these features are enabled. Modifying these settings can affect resource pack generation, so reinstalling the resource pack may be necessary if you experience issues.
        
    

Copy

    modules:
      nameplates: true
      backgrounds: true
      bubbles: true
      bossbars: true
      actionbars: true
      images: true

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/config.yml#plugin-integrations)

**Plugin Integrations:**

*   **resource-pack:** Here, you can choose whether to integrate resource packs from specific plugins like `ItemsAdder` and `Oraxen`.
    
*   **chat integrations:** Supported chat plugins can be integrated for features like blacklist channels and ignoring functionality.
    

Copy

    integrations:
      resource-pack: ...
      chat: ...

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/config.yml#resource-pack-generation-settings)

**Resource Pack Generation Settings:**

*   **disable-generation-on-start:** Set to `false`, allowing resource pack generation when the server starts.
    
*   **namespace:** This field defines the namespace for your resource pack, here set to `"nameplates"`.
    
*   **font:** Specifies which font to use. The default font is set to `"default"`.
    
*   **initial-char:** Defines the starting character for custom fonts. Here, `뀁` is used, which won't affect normal Korean characters during chat.
    
*   **image-path:** Specifies where the PNG files for various assets (nameplates, backgrounds, images, etc.) will be generated. These paths help maintain an organized resource pack structure.
    
*   **transparent-bossbar:** Settings for generating transparent bossbars
    
*   **legacy-unicodes:** Enables support for legacy Unicode characters in Minecraft 1.20+ clients, adding approximately 900KB to your resource pack size.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/config.yml#additional-settings)

**Additional Settings:**

*   **legacy-color-code-support:** Enables support for legacy Minecraft color codes (using `&`). Disabling this can improve color formatting performance.
    
*   **send-delay:** Specifies a delay for actionbar/bossbar to ensure compatibility with other plugins.
    
*   **catch-other-plugin-actionbar:** Set to `true` to capture actionbars from other plugins.
    
*   **unsafe-chat-event:** Set to whether the plugin should listen for chat events canceled by unknown plugins.
    
*   **refresh intervals:** Defines the default refresh intervals for conditions and placeholders.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/config.yml#font-templates)

**Font Templates:**

*   **font-templates:** This section defines how the system loads different fonts, such as `space`, `unihex`, and `bitmap` fonts. You can add new configurations here or replace existing font templates. It manages the various character types provided by [Minecraft Font Providersarrow-up-right](https://minecraft.wiki/w/Font#Providers)
    
*   **Font Configuration Options:**
    
    *   `file`: Refers to a file located in the `/CustomNameplates/font` directory.
        
    *   `custom`: Specifies whether to use the default PNG bitmap font provided by the client.
        
    *   `generate`: Indicates whether to include a copy of this font in the generated resource pack.
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/config.yml#shift-fonts)

**Shift fonts:**

See [Shift Text](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/shift-text)

[Previous⚙️ Configchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config)
[Nextbossbar.ymlchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/config/bossbar.yml)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    resource-pack:
      disable-generation-on-start: false
      namespace: "nameplates"
      font: "default"
      initial-char: '뀁'
      image-path:
        nameplates: 'font/nameplates/'
        backgrounds: 'font/backgrounds/'
        images: 'font/images/'
        bubbles: 'font/bubbles/'
        space-split: 'font/base/'
      shader:
        enable: true
        hide-scoreboard-number: false # 1.19.4 - 1.20.3
        animated-text: false
        ItemsAdder-text-effects: false
      transparent-bossbar:
        color: YELLOW
        "1_20_2+": true
        "1_17-1_20_1": true
      legacy-unicodes: true

Copy

    other-settings:
      legacy-color-code-support: true
      send-delay: 0
      catch-other-plugin-actionbar: true
      unsafe-chat-event: false
      default-condition-refresh-interval: 1
      default-placeholder-refresh-interval: 1
      placeholder-refresh-interval:
        "%player_name%": 100
        "%vault_prefix%": 1

Copy

    other-settings:
      font-templates:
        space:
          space:
            ' ': 4
            ‌: 0
        unihex:
          unifont:
            file: "unifont.zip"
            generate: false
            size_overrides:
            - from: "、"
              to: "ヿ"
              left: 0
              right: 15
            - from: "㈀"
              to: "鿿"
              left: 0
              right: 15
            - from: "ᄀ"
              to: "ᇿ"
              left: 0
              right: 15
            - from: "㄰"
              to: "㆏"
              left: 0
              right: 15
            - from: "ꥠ"
              to: "꥿"
              left: 0
              right: 15
            - from: "ힰ"
              to: "퟿"
              left: 0
              right: 15
            - from: "가"
              to: "힯"
              left: 1
              right: 15
            - from: "豈"
              to: "﫿"
              left: 0
              right: 15
            - from: "！"
              to: "～"
              left: 0
              right: 15

            file: "unifont_jp.zip"
            generate: false

              jp: true
            size_overrides:
            - from: "㈀"
              to: "鿿"
              left: 0

              to: "﫿"

            height: 8

          ascii_sga:
            codepoints: "ascii_sga"
            file: "ascii_sga.png"
            height: 8
            custom: false
          asciillager:
            codepoints: "asciillager"
            file: "asciillager.png"
            height: 8
            custom: false
          nonlatin_european:
            codepoints: "nonlatin_european"
            file: "nonlatin_european.png"
            height: 8
            custom: false
          accented:

            file: "accented.png"
            height: 12
            custom: false
        legacy_unicode:
          legacy_unicode:
            file: "unicode_page_%02x.png"
            height: 8
            custom: false
        unicode:
          unicode:
            file: "unicode_page_%02x.png"
            sizes: "glyph_sizes.bin"
        ttf:
          example:
            generate: false
            file: "example.ttf"
            size: 10.0
            oversample: 8.0
            skip: []
