# ❓️ Common Questions | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q1-purple-bossbars)

Q1: Purple bossbars

The default bossbar in plugin should be Yellow. If you see a purple bossbar, it's a bug in Lunar Client.

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q2-how-to-use-images-from-itemsadder-oraxen)

Q2: How to use Images from ItemsAdder/Oraxen

You should surround your images with font tags for instance

Copy

    <font:minecraft:default>%img_xxx%</font>  # Don't forget to close the tag

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q3-the-background-doesnt-fit-the-text)

Q3: The background doesn't fit the text

This is because the plugin doesn't know the advance(width) of your custom images. Images registered in CustomNameplates would fit the background but if you are using another plugin for instance ItemsAdder to create new images, you should input your images' advance at **/configs/advance-data.yml.**

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FCqZNsGY1ENwH3UJBlX1T%2F7D1A659B809DDD22F34A11C576B142D6.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=169f5fc8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q4-im-using-a-custom-bitmap-font)

Q4: I'm using a custom bitmap font

If you are using a custom font through bitmap, just put it into plugin's /font folder and override the previous one. Then delete the `/tmp` folder from the plugin folder. At last, restart the server.

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FjxB13fEqolZBS3m565da%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=94010eef&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q5-whats-the-black-square)

Q5: What's the black square?

This is caused by ItemsAdder hud. Just disable it in ItemsAdder config.yml

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FJXucpqyIFn23Qiju9Zn2%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=759d5da2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q6-i-want-to-move-the-image-down-up)

Q6: I want to move the image down/up

If the image is registered by CustomNameplates, simply edit the `ascent` option.

You can't move the image down/up from CustomNameplates side if you are using an image from other plugins. Actually it's easy to fix because in those plugins they provide an option to edit the image's ascent (In ItemsAdder it's called `y_position`)

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2F030uofho8ddLagCgfytx%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6631fef3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q7-players-cant-see-bossbar)

Q7: Players can't see bossbar

You should give them permission "bossbar.show" or remove the permission condition from bossbar configs.

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q8-bubbles-not-working)

Q8: Bubbles not working

This is because any chat plugin would cancel the player chat event. To solve that, firstly check if the plugin is officially supported in config.yml and enable the integration if available

If you are using an unsupported plugin, you can make a suggestion, but only if that plugin has an API repository. The worst solution is to turn on `unsafe-chat-event` in config.yml

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q9-bossbar-conflicts-with-hud-plugins)

Q9: Bossbar conflicts with HUD plugins

Setting `send-delay` to a proper value in config.yml would fix

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q10-shader-conflicts)

Q10: Shader conflicts

If you encounter shader conflicts, you will need to either merge the shaders (which requires some GLSL knowledge) or disable the CustomNameplates shader.

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q11-super-dark-background)

Q11: Super dark background

If you notice that your background color is unusually dark, it means the shader has not been successfully applied to your client. This is usually caused by a shader conflict, as the client can only apply one shader at a time. If you need to use multiple shaders, you'll have to manually merge them. If you're unable to resolve the issue, you can consider reducing the opacity of the image as an alternative solution. This can help mitigate the visual impact of the shader conflict.

(Alternative images can be downloaded here. To use, replace the ones under /contents/backgrounds/ folder)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q12-player-names-are-displayed-like)

Q12: Player names are displayed like “□□□□”

This issue occurs because **unifont\_jp** cannot be read by clients running versions 1.19.4 to 1.20.3, and **unifont** cannot be read by 1.19.4 clients. This means that compatibility between certain fonts and specific Minecraft versions may lead to display issues.

If you're running a 1.20+ server, you can consider removing **unifont\_jp** as shown in the example below if you don't really need it:

If you're running a 1.19.4 server, you can configure as shown in the example below:

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2Ft4I4HuGeogJULTMOBL9W%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7802791&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/common-questions#q13-how-to-use-ttf-fonts)

Q13: How to use TTF fonts

Uncomment the ttf section in `config.yml` and replace `example` with the font name you use. Then put your TTF file under `/CustomNameplates/font` and restart your server.

Then you are allowed to use ttf in shift-fonts

Please note that ttf text advance calculations may not be accurate. Therefore it is not currently recommended for very large fonts. If you find that the advance of a certain character is incorrect, you can use a text editor to edit the advance data of the corresponding character in `/tmp/xxx.tmp(Requires a restart to apply)`

[Next📖 Basic Font Knowledgechevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/basic-font-knowledge)

        file: example.ttf             # Define the TTF file to load the font from
        size: 10.0                    # Set font size
        oversample: 8.0               # Oversample rate for TTF rendering
        skip: []                      # Skipped characters in list format

    shift_3:
      - space
      - example:3  # the number here is the Y shift

# Background/Nameplate/Bubble Text | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

The `background-text` provides a border that adjusts to the width of the text. You can control whether it has a shadow using the `shadow` option, and adjust the left and right margins using the `margin` option. This allows for a fully customizable background appearance, giving you precise control over text presentation.

Copy

    background-text:
      weather:
        background: bedrock_1
        text: '%np_image_weather% %np_shift_weather%'
        shadow: false
        left-margin: 1
        right-margin: 1

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FeHZsZupKEk6l9ZnAttbl%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4334f7de&sv=2)

shadow: false

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2F8lUDxmw6wKUreJp3quNT%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1a3f1466&sv=2)

shadow: true

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FlL33SseSU7PKIl1LEvpV%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89ab3ab2&sv=2)

right-margin: 20

**Nameplate-text** and **Bubble-text** work in a similar way, providing flexible control over text formatting and display. Below is how they function:

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2F2kfe1GCXD0dxQNl6hNR7%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=acc7844b&sv=2)

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FUqXKcv4uYjwj1OzB9YjO%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dbed02d4&sv=2)

[PreviousSwitch Textchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/switch-text)

        right-margin: 1

        bubble: chat_1

# ✏️ Text | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

The plugin employs the `MiniMessage` ([https://docs.advntr.dev/minimessage/format.htmlarrow-up-right](https://docs.advntr.dev/minimessage/format.html)
) format for text representation. This system provides a rich and flexible way to format text with colors, styles, and other features. However, if you're more comfortable with or require the old color format (using the '&' symbol), it's still supported.

#### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/text#legacy-color-code-support)

Legacy Color Code Support:

Here's how it should look in the `config.yml`:

To enable the support for the legacy color format:

Copy

    other-settings:
      legacy-color-code-support: true

# Shift Text | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

**shift-text** provides vertical offset for text. The default configuration applies a slight downward shift to better align the text with the background positioning. This ensures that the text is displayed in harmony with other visual elements, such as nameplates or bubbles, improving overall aesthetic consistency.

Copy

    # /configs/custom-placeholder.yml
    shift-text:
      weather:
        text: "Weather: %np_conditional_weather%"
        font: shift_1

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FSlVQSEVMVhxyDkmggWmW%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=14839f6b&sv=2)

Fonts are registered within the `config.yml` file. Here are a few examples to demonstrate how this system works:

Using **shift\_1** as an example, if the `ascii` font has a height of 8 pixels (font image height) and an ascent of 3, it means the text is shifted downward by 5 pixels relative to its normal position. This downward offset is calculated as the difference between the height and ascent (`8 - 3 = 5`), meaning the text will appear lower than usual to align with other elements.

Here’s an example of the **default height** configuration for fonts in `config.yml`:

For the **accented** font, due to its larger height, a higher ascent value is used to maintain proper alignment. In this case, an ascent of 6 is applied instead of 3, balancing the larger font height for accented characters.

By adjusting the values in the configuration, you'll notice a clear visual difference in how the text is rendered. Here’s an example of how these adjustments might look: (Please note that after making these adjustments, you'll need to **reload your resource pack** for the changes to take effect! This ensures that all the new font settings, such as the updated heights and ascents, are properly applied and reflected in-game.)

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FEMkoUJwxjq1Ok8jyzMJc%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=81b3b03f&sv=2)

ascii:3

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FdZMmdez4xY6ewo89gGF9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=547b9fe3&sv=2)

ascii:-15

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FddWt9eXwVM4Zl7VSG9Pg%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=665f0b76&sv=2)

ascii:-30

When using this in practice, you only need to select the specific character sets you plan to use and create offset fonts accordingly. This approach minimizes the size of the resource pack by avoiding the inclusion of unnecessary character sets, leading to better performance and faster loading times.

In the default configuration, since only numbers are used for displaying gold, `money` uses `shift_2` and selected the ASCII character set. This efficiently minimizes the resource pack by only including the necessary characters for the money display.

[PreviousBackground/Nameplate/Bubble Textchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/background-nameplate-bubble-text)
[NextConditional Textchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/conditional-text)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    # config.yml
    shift-fonts:
      shift_1:
      - "space"
      - "nonlatin_european:3"
      - "accented:6"
      - "ascii:3"
      - "legacy_unicode:3"

Copy

    ascii: 8
    ascii_sga: 8
    asciillager: 8
    nonlatin_european: 8
    accented: 12

Copy

    shift_1:
    - "space"
    - "nonlatin_european:3"
    - "accented:6"
    - "ascii:-15"
    - "legacy_unicode:3"

Copy

    shift_1:
    - "space"
    - "nonlatin_european:3"
    - "accented:6"
    - "ascii:-30"
    - "legacy_unicode:3"

Copy

    # config.yml
    shift-fonts:
      shift_2:
      - "space"
      - "ascii:-15"

Copy

    # /configs/custom-placeholder.yml
    shift-text:
      money:
        text: "%vault_eco_balance%"
        font: shift_2

# 🦖 Entity | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

Entity configuration is straightforward. It only requires an ID and a velocity setting. Depending on the entity you are using, some plugins allow the use of properties.

[ItemsAdderchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/compatibility/itemsadder)
[MythicMobschevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/compatibility/mythicmobs)

Copy

    skeleton:
      entity: skeleton
      velocity:
        horizontal: 1
        vertical: 1.3
      properties: {}

**Entity ID**: A unique identifier for each entity. This ensures the game or plugin can recognize and differentiate between various entities.

**Velocity**: This refers to the speed of an entity's movement when getting out of water surface.

**Properties**: These are additional settings that can define an entity's behavior, appearance, or other characteristics. The available properties can vary based on the type of entity and the specific plugin in use.

[Previous🎁 Itemchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/item)
[Next🧊 Blockchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/block)

# 🕹️ MiniGame | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

Mini game config has these two properties that would apply for all game types: **difficulty & time**

Copy

    # The difficulty of the game (1~100) (EFAULT VALUE: "20~80")
    difficulty: 15~30  
    difficulty: 50
    
    # Maximum allowed game time in seconds (DEFAULT VALUE: 15)
    time: 15~25
    time: 15

Mini games provide fun for fishing and can to some extent prevent players from using automatic fishing. Here are the inbuilt game types:

# 🧊 Block | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

The fishing plugin introduces a unique feature that enables players to fish up blocks! This isn't limited to vanilla blocks or the default fishing loots. The plugin seamlessly integrates with other plugins, allowing users to set up custom blocks. One of the highlights of this feature is the capability to fish up chests filled with randomized items, making every catch a potential surprise!

Copy

    apple_crate:
      block: barrel
      velocity:
        horizontal: 1.07
        vertical: 1.5
      properties:
        directional: true
        storage:
          apple_1:
            item: APPLE
            amount: 1~2
            chance: 0.8
          apple_2:
            item: APPLE
            amount: 1~2
            chance: 0.8

**Block Type:** Define the type of block. In this case, it's a barrel.

**Velocity**: This refers to the speed of the block's movement when getting out of water surface.

**Properties:** Configure the behavior and characteristics of the block.

**Available properties:**

[Previous🦖 Entitychevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/entity)
[Next🏆 Lootchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/loot)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    directional-4: true
    
    directional-6: true
    
    moisture: 4
    
    campfire: true
    
    rotatable: true
    
    noteblock:
      instrument: PIANO
      note: 7
    
    age: 4
    
    turtle-eggs: 3
    
    storage:
      apple_1:
        # Tip: To use Custom Fishing items, just input "CustomFishing:type:id"
        item: APPLE
        amount: 1~2
        chance: 0.8

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Click | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fi.imgur.com%2FhxHnhyC.gif&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bba88525&sv=2)

Copy

    click_game:
      game-type: click
      difficulty: 40~60  # amount of click
      time: 15
      left-click: true # true = left click / false = right click
      title: '<red>{progress}'
      subtitle: "<gray>Left click <white>{clicks} <gray>times to win. Time left <white>{time_left}s"

# ItemsAdder | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

For items:

Copy

    material: ItemsAdder:namespace:id

For blocks:

Copy

    block: ItemsAdder:namespace:id

For mobs:

Copy

    mob: ItemsAdder:namespace:id
    properties:
      frustumCulling: false  # if this entity needs to be frozen if not visible by the player.
      noBase: false  # if this custom entity doesn't have a Bukkit real entity as base
      noHitbox: false  # if this custom entity bones have the armorstands hitboxes or not

[Previous🤝 Compatibilitychevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/compatibility)

        font: 'customfishing:default'
        bar: '뀑'

        struggling-fish:
          - 뀎
          - 뀏
          - 뀎
          - 뀐

        fish-offset: -221
        fish-start-position: 165
        fish-icon-width: 8
        success-position: 21
        ultimate-tension: 50
        normal-pull-tension-increase: 1
        struggling-tension-increase: 2
        loosening-tension-loss: 2
      tension:
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀑</font>'
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀒</font>'
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀓</font>'
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀔</font>'

# Dance | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fi.imgur.com%2FeRrMZrn.gif&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fde899f7&sv=2)

Copy

    dance_game:
      game-type: dance
      difficulty: 40~60 # (The amount of buttons would be difficulty/4)
      time: 15
      easy: true # (true = ←→ / false = ←→↑↓)
      tip: '<gray>↑: Jump | ↓: Sneak | ←: LeftClick | →: RightClick</gray>'
      title: 
        left-button: '<gray>← </gray>'
        left-button-correct: '<green>← </green>'
        left-button-wrong: '<red>← </red>'
        left-button-current: '<gold>← </gold>'
        right-button: '<gray>→ </gray>'
        right-button-correct: '<green>→ </green>'
        right-button-wrong: '<red>→ </red>'
        right-button-current: '<gold>→ </gold>'
        up-button: '<gray>↑ </gray>'
        up-button-correct: '<green>↑ </green>'
        up-button-wrong: '<red>↑ </red>'
        up-button-current: '<gold>↑ </gold>'
        down-button: '<gray>↓ </gray>'
        down-button-correct: '<green>↓ </green>'
        down-button-wrong: '<red>↓ </red>'
        down-button-current: '<gold>↓ </gold>'
        display-amount: 7 # (Max amount of buttons to be displayed at the same time)
      subtitle: "<gray>Dance to win. Time left <white>{time_left}s"
      sound:
        correct: "minecraft:block.amethyst_block.hit"
        wrong: "minecraft:block.anvil.land"

[PreviousClickchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/minigame/click)
[Next🏅 Competitionchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/competition)

then add it loot-conditions.yml

     - mcmmo:+10

# Side Money Bar | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2449012911-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%252Fuploads%252F3110UME9ks74gmTtpguQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D784310d7-6a70-408b-91a8-a2b26ef02002&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=28efcc7a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/examples/side-money-bar#tutorial)

Tutorial

First, we need to prepare a new background configuration. Please place the following content into the plugin's `contents/background` folder.

file-archive

7KB

[backgrounds.zip](https://2449012911-files.gitbook.io/~/files/v0/b/gitbook-x-prod.appspot.com/o/spaces%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fuploads%2F1k3jweXmXvYKy1eCBo3E%2Fbackgrounds.zip?alt=media&token=77e180bf-f46a-412f-bcd3-39e47b33c493)

archive

downloadDownload[arrow-up-right-from-squareOpen](https://2449012911-files.gitbook.io/~/files/v0/b/gitbook-x-prod.appspot.com/o/spaces%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fuploads%2F1k3jweXmXvYKy1eCBo3E%2Fbackgrounds.zip?alt=media&token=77e180bf-f46a-412f-bcd3-39e47b33c493)

Secondly open your `/contents/images/coin.yml` file and modify the `ascent` value to a lower position.

Then add a new shift font in `config.yml`

At last open `configs/custom-placeholders.yml` and add or modify the configuration as follows:

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/examples/side-money-bar#tips)

Tips

If you want to add another line, such as the player's points, simply follow the same steps as above: create a new background, shift-font, and image configuration, but with a smaller ascent value.

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2449012911-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%252Fuploads%252FmeXVo3vVfZfGFW5n3Kzv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3066847-cabc-49e8-9dc7-799dc49acca1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0ba6570&sv=2)

If you don't need a background, simply replace the `background-text` variable with the `shift-text` variable.

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2449012911-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%252Fuploads%252FuBLUbKC5ccpURBUUbl9C%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5fc92d0a-1e5d-4ee3-bf4a-e39d9ca11bf9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5a96bfe&sv=2)

Of course, you can also use a custom font if you think it looks better. Just don't forget to create a more compact background and icon.

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2449012911-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%252Fuploads%252FfIHwQxN1ANGTox6q17f7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30c2437c-cae9-4413-a5e4-4c1657ede6c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b57168e&sv=2)

Copy

    image: coin
    height: 10
    ascent: -40
    shadow: false

Copy

    other-settings:
      shift-fonts:
        shift_3:
        - "space"
        - "ascii:-41"

Copy

    conditional-text:
      actionbar:
        priority_1:
          text: '%np_background_other_actionbar%' # hides the money hud when a player is other game mode
          conditions:
            condition_or:
              type: "||"
              refresh-interval: 1
              value:
                condition_gamemode:
                  type: "!gamemode"
                  refresh-interval: 1
                  value: survival
        priority_2:
          text: '%np_static_other_actionbar%%np_static_money_hud%' # displays the money hud + other plugin's actionbar message
          conditions:
            condition_other_actionbar:
              type: "!equals"
              refresh-interval: 1
              value:
                value1: '%np_actionbar%'
                value2: ""
        priority_3:
          text: '%np_offset_210%%np_static_money_hud%' # displays the money hud only

Copy

    background-text:
      money_hud:
        background: black
        text: '%np_shift_money%'
        shadow: false
        left-margin: 4
        right-margin: 1

Copy

    static-text:
      money_part:
        position: left
        text: '%np_background_money_hud%'
        value: 0
      money_hud:
        position: left
        text: '%np_static_money_part%<!shadow>%np_offset_-6%%np_image_coin%</!shadow>'
        value: 0
      other_actionbar:
        position: middle
        text: "%np_background_other_actionbar%"
        value: 210

Copy

    shift-text:
      money:
        text: "100.0k"
        font: shift_3

Copy

    conditional-text:
      actionbar:
        priority_1:
          text: '%np_background_other_actionbar%' # hides the hud when a player is other game mode
          conditions:
            condition_or:
              type: "||"
              refresh-interval: 1
              value:
                condition_gamemode:
                  type: "!gamemode"
                  refresh-interval: 1
                  value: survival
        priority_2:
          text: '%np_static_other_actionbar%%np_static_money_hud%%np_static_point_hud%' # displays the money hud + point hud + other plugin's actionbar message
          conditions:
            condition_other_actionbar:
              type: "!equals"
              refresh-interval: 1
              value:
                value1: '%np_actionbar%'
                value2: ""
        priority_3:
          text: '%np_offset_210%%np_static_money_hud%%np_static_point_hud%' # displays the money hud and the point hud

Copy

    background-text:
      point_hud:
        background: black_2  # You'll need to create this background
        text: '%np_shift_point%'
        shadow: false
        left-margin: 4
        right-margin: 1

Copy

    static-text:
      point_part:
        position: left
        text: '%np_background_point_hud%'
        value: 0
      point_hud:
        position: left
        text: '%np_static_point_part%<!shadow>%np_offset_-6%%np_image_bell%</!shadow>'
        value: 0

Copy

    shift-text:
      point:
        text: "12345"
        font: shift_4  # You'll need to create this shift font

Copy

    static-text:
      money_part:
        position: left
        text: '%np_shift_money%'
        value: 0
      point_part:
        position: left
        text: '%np_shift_point%'
        value: 0
      money_hud:
        position: left
        text: '<!shadow>%np_image_coin%</!shadow>%np_static_money_part%'
        value: 0
      point_hud:
        position: left
        text: '<!shadow>%np_image_bell%</!shadow>%np_static_point_part%'
        value: 0

# Basic Operations | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/api/basic-operations#get-api-instance)

Get API instance

Copy

    CustomNameplatesAPI api = CustomNameplatesAPI.getInstance();

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/api/basic-operations#create-text-with-images)

Create text with images

Copy

    Optional<Background> background = api.getBackground("bedrock_1");
    if (background.isPresent()) {
        String textWithBackground = api.createTextWithImage("<red>Test Message</red>", background.get(), 1, 1);
    }

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/api/basic-operations#subscribe-events)

Subscribe events

Copy

    CustomNameplates.getInstance().getEventManager().subscribe(CommandFeedbackEvent.class, event -> {
        if (event.key().equals("xxx.xxx")) {
            if (event.sender() instanceof Player player) {
                event.cancelled(true);
                player.sendActionBar("xxxxxxx");
            }
        }
    });

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/api/basic-operations#get-the-advance-of-the-text)

Get the advance of the text

*   [Get API instance](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/api/basic-operations#get-api-instance)

# ClueScrolls | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

Copy

    common_1:
       lore: '&a★ &fCatch %amount% fish: %completed%'
       clueType: customfishing_loot
       amount: 7-15
       objective: Catch %amount% tuna fish
       clueName: Fisherman
       data:
         id: tuna_fish  <- specific loot
         id: any        <- any loot
    
    common_2:
       lore: '&a★ &fCatch %amount% golden star fish: %completed%'
       clueType: customfishing_group
       amount: 7-15
       objective: Catch %amount% golden star fish
       clueName: Fisherman
       data:
         group: golden_star

Copy

    hold_game_easy:
      game-type: hold_v2
      difficulty: 100
      time: 15
      title: '{progress}'
      left-click: true # true = left click / false = right-click
      # Tip would show on the title to guide the player how to play
      tip: '<gray>Press <red><key:key.mouse.left> <gray>to start'
      subtitle:
        font: 'customfishing:default'
        bar: '뀌'
        judgment-area: '뀒'
        pointer: '뀁'
      arguments:
        punishment: 0.2
        bar-effective-area-width: 155
        judgment-area-offset: -160
        judgment-area-width: 45
        pointer-icon-width: 5
        water-resistance: 0.15
        pulling-strength: 3
        loosening-strength-loss: 0.5
        elasticity: false
        elasticity-power: 0.7
      hold-time-requirements:
        - 3
        - 3
        - 4
      progress:
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀁</font>'
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀂</font>'
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀃</font>'
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀄</font>'
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀅</font>'
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀆</font>'
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀇</font>'
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀈</font>'
        - '<font:customfishing:icons>뀉</font>'

# 🅿️ Placeholders | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/placeholders#common-placeholders)

Common Placeholders

If you want to use with PlaceholderAPI in other plugins, simply replace `%np_` with `%nameplates_`. (e.g. `%nameplates_offset_30%`)

If this is a nested placeholder and contains relational placeholders, add `%rel_` before the placeholder. (e.g. `%rel_np_conditional_friend%`)

If this placeholder is shared by all players, you can add `%shared_` before the placeholder to improve performance (e.g. `%shared_customcrops_season_world%`)

placeholder

value

%player\_name%

player name

%player\_x%

x coordinate

%player\_y%

y coordinate

%player\_z%

z coordinate

%player\_world%

world name

%player\_remaining\_air%

the remaining oxygen

%np\_offset\_\[-256~256\]%

generate offset characters

%np\_tag-image%

nameplate image

%np\_tag-text%

nameplate text

%np\_tag%

full nameplate tag

%np\_equipped\_nameplate%

id of the equipped nameplate

%np\_equipped\_nameplate-name%

display name of the equipped nameplate

%np\_equipped\_bubble%

id of the equipped bubble

%np\_equipped\_bubble-name%

display name of the equipped bubble

%np\_is-latest%

check if the plugin is the latest

%np\_gradient\_\[1~20\]%

generate gradient offset numbers based on speed (1~20)

%np\_time\_12%

time in 12-hour format

%np\_time\_24%

time in 24-hour format

%np\_biome%

id of the biome

%np\_actionbar%

actionbar message from other plugins or commands

%np\_image\_\[id\]%

the image registered in CustomNameplates

%np\_img\_\[id\]%

the raw image character

%np\_is\_showing%

gets whether the player has used the toggle command to display the tag (true/false)

%np\_is\_previewing%

gets whether the player is previewing the tag (true/false)

%np\_conditional\_\[id\]%

[Conditional Text](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/conditional-text)

%np\_background\_\[id\]%

%np\_background-text\_\[id\]%

%np\_background-image\_\[id\]%

[Background/Nameplate/Bubble Text](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/background-nameplate-bubble-text)

%np\_nameplate\_\[id\]% %np\_nameplate-text\_\[id\]% %np\_nameplate-image\_\[id\]%

[Background/Nameplate/Bubble Text](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/background-nameplate-bubble-text)

%np\_bubble\_\[id\]% %np\_bubble-text\_\[id\]% %np\_bubble-image\_\[id\]%

[Background/Nameplate/Bubble Text](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/background-nameplate-bubble-text)

%np\_switch\_\[id\]%

[Switch Text](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/switch-text)

%np\_vanilla\_\[id\]%

[Vanilla Hud](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/vanilla-hud)

%np\_static\_\[id\]%

[Static Text](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/static-text)

%np\_shift\_\[id\]%

[Shift Text](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/custom-placeholders/shift-text)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/placeholders#extra-placeholders)

Extra Placeholders

Extra placeholders are additional variables provided by the plugin. These variables are currently only available after the PlaceholderAPI is installed, which provides some useful functions.

placeholder

value

%npex\_offset\_\[number\]%

generate offset characters

%npex\_lunarphase\_\[world\]%

gets the lunar phase in the specified world

%npex\_lunarphase%

gets the lunar phase in the world player in

%npex\_weather\_\[world\]%

gets the weather in the specified world

%npex\_weather%

gets the weather in the world player in

%npex\_time12\_\[world\]%

time in 12-hour format

%npex\_time12%

time in 12-hour format

%npex\_time24\_\[world\]%

time in 24-hour format

%npex\_time24%

time in 24-hour format

%npex\_background\_\[id\]:\[left-margin\]:\[right-margin\]:\[width\]%

generates a background based on the given parameters Example: %npex\_background\_bedrock\_1:1:1:20%

%npex\_newline%

returns \\n

%npex\_smallfont\_\[placeholder/text\]%

gets the text in small font

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2Fg4wtRrMAjHLwLx4VVuoA%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30f7f90c&sv=2)

%npex\_static\_\[position\]:\[value\]:\[text\]%

create a static text (position = left,right,middle)

# Stamina Bar | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

before:

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FOnbt1sSS30qH4Txz8AxR%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b088dfe6&sv=2)

after:

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2Fe1UZDdIzlJTUqQBtqN7u%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb2163f6&sv=2)

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FbuTaLtsxDmiwj5OFuCMf%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a81cf687&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/examples/stamina-bar#step-1)

Step 1


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Move the image and text up

Now reload the plugin and reinstall the resource pack to see the changes

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2Fjf7LPT1kv6trPpHJ1vQz%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb9238dd&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/examples/stamina-bar#step-2)

Step 2


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Default config hides the money when players are in water but in this case we don't have to hide it

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FRgjUtzZWTyu9Uner0nJe%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1dbc894f&sv=2)

Now reload the configs and see the result

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FK4cBhAa5pxZPyaxUrwgx%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=542d9172&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/examples/stamina-bar#step-3)

Step 3


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add stamina bar

Method 1: Since we know that the width of this hud is fixed, we can use `%nameplates_offset_100%%nameplates_vanilla_stamina_hud%` to add another line

Method 2: We can also use static text

    # before

          conditions:
            '||':
              '!=':
                value1: '%player_remaining_air%'
                value2: "300"
              '!gamemode': survival
        priority_2:
          text: '%np_static_money_hud%%np_offset_-179%%np_static_other_actionbar%'
          conditions:
            '!equals':
              value1: '%np_actionbar%'
              value2: ""
        priority_3:
          text: '%np_static_money_hud%'
    
    # after
    conditional-text:
      actionbar:
        priority_1:
          text: '%np_static_money_hud%%np_offset_-180%%np_static_other_actionbar%'
          conditions:
            '||':
              '!=':
                value1: '%player_remaining_air%'
                value2: "300"
              '!gamemode': survival
        priority_2:
          text: '%np_static_money_hud%%np_offset_-180%%np_static_other_actionbar%'
          conditions:
            '!equals':
              value1: '%np_actionbar%'
              value2: ""
        priority_3:
          text: '%np_static_money_hud%'

Copy

    conditional-text:
      actionbar:
        priority_1:
          text: '%np_static_money_hud%%np_offset_-180%%np_static_other_actionbar%'
          conditions:
            '||':
              '!=':
                value1: '%player_remaining_air%'
                value2: "300"
              '!gamemode': survival
        priority_2:
          text: '%np_offset_100%%np_vanilla_stamina_hud%%np_offset_-180%%np_static_money_hud%%np_offset_-180%%np_static_other_actionbar%'
          conditions:
            '!equals':
              value1: '%np_actionbar%'
              value2: ""
        priority_3:
          text: '%np_offset_100%%np_vanilla_stamina_hud%%np_offset_-180%%np_static_money_hud%'

Copy

    static-text:
      stamina_hud:
        position: right
        text: '%np_vanilla_stamina_hud%'
        value: 180

Copy

# 🎉 Event | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/event#introduction)

Introduction

Events are the prerequisites that trigger actions. This article will detail all the configuration areas where events can be applied. Here's a simple example where players are given experience orbs on successful fishing

Copy

    #contents/item/default.yml
    tuna_fish:
      events:
        success:  # trigger
          action_mending:  # actions
            type: mending
            value: 5
            chance: 1.0

All the available action types can be found on

[💪 Actionchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/action)

Here are the available triggers for different mechanics

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/event#loots)

Loots

Copy

    events:
      success:   <- successful loot capture
       ...
      failure:   <- failed loot capture
       ...
      hook:      <- fish hooked (Requires reeling in)
       ...
      success-times:
        1:       <- number of successful loot captures
         ...
        2:
         ...
        999:
         ...
      consume:   <- ate by player
        ...
      bite:      <- fish attempt to eat the hook
        ...
      new_size_record:   <- the size of fish caught exceeded personal record
        ... 
      interact:   <- interact with the item in hand
        ...

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/event#rods)

Rods

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/event#baits)

Baits

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/event#utils)

Utils

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/event#totems)

Totems

[Previous✨ Effectchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect)
[Next✏️ Textchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/text)

*   [Introduction](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/event#introduction)

# 🛒 Market | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

**Enable Feature:**

*   `enable: true` This toggles whether the entire feature is enabled or disabled.
    

Copy

    enable: true

**Container Title:**

*   `title: '<gradient:#A52A2A:#800000:#A52A2A>Fish Market</gradient>'` This specifies the title of the container. The title "Fish Market" is displayed with a gradient color effect transitioning between three given hex color codes.
    

Copy

    title: '<gradient:#A52A2A:#800000:#A52A2A>Fish Market</gradient>'

Copy

    # Change title dynamically (since2.3.2)
    titles:
      deny: xxx
      limit: xxx
      allow: xxx

**Limitation:**

*   `limitation:` This section defines the limitations related to earnings from the fish market.
    
    *   `enable: true` means the limitation feature is turned on.
        
    *   `earnings: 10000` specifies a cap on earnings at 10,000 units.
        
    

Copy

    limitation:
      enable: true
      earnings: 10000
      # Support expression and placeholders
      earnings: '1000 + 50 * {level}'

**Market Menu Layout:**

*   `layout:` The layout section determines the visual arrangement of items/icons within the market menu. The symbols 'A', 'I', and 'B' reference specific items or icons.
    

**Price Formula:**

*   `price-formula: '{base} + {bonus} * {size}'` This provides a formula to calculate the price of loots from "CustomFishing".
    

**Item Price:**

*   `item-price:` This segment assigns fixed prices to items. For instance, the "COD" is priced at 10 units. Additionally, items with a `CustomModelData` like "PAPER" with data "999" is priced at 5 units.
    

**Item Slot:**

*   `item-slot:` Dictates the slot where items (symbolized as 'I') to sell are placed. Items without an assigned price can still be placed if `allow-items-with-no-price` is set to true.
    

**Dynamic Icons: (sell-icons / sell-all-icons)** This section manages interactive icons. Icons here have multiple functions:

*   `allow-icon`: Indicates permitted trades.
    
*   `deny-icon`: Represents denied trades due to a lack of items to sell.
    
*   `limit-icon`: Appears when the worth of items exceeds the daily earnable amount. Each icon is further configured with display settings and triggered actions, such as sounds, messages, or commands.
    

**Decorative Icons:**

*   `decorative-icons:` These icons are purely for visual enhancement. They do not possess functional attributes. In this case, a `glass-pane` is assigned symbol 'A', with the material being `BLACK_STAINED_GLASS_PANE`.
    

[Previous📄 Formatchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format)
[Next✨ Effectchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    layout:
      - 'AAAAAAAAA'
      - 'AIIIIIIIA'
      - 'AIIIIIIIA'
      - 'AIIIIIIIA'
      - 'AAAABAAAA'

Copy

    price-formula: '{base} + {bonus} * {size}'

Copy

    item-price:
      COD: 10
      PUFFERFISH: 10
      SALMON: 10
      TROPICAL_FISH: 10
      PAPER:999: 5

Copy

    item-slot:
      symbol: 'I'
      allow-items-with-no-price: true

Copy

    sell-all-icons:
      ...
    sell-icons:
      symbol: 'B'
      allow-icon:
        material: IRON_BLOCK
        display:
          name: '<#00CED1><b>● <!b>Ship the fish'
          lore:
            - '<font:uniform><gradient:#E6E6FA:#48D1CC:#E6E6FA>You will get <green>{money}$</green> by selling the fish</gradient></font>'
            - '<dark_gray>You can earn {rest}'
        action:
          sound_action:
            type: sound
            value:
              key: 'minecraft:block.amethyst_block.place'
              source: 'player'
              volume: 1
              pitch: 1
          message_action:
            type: message
            value: 'You earned {money}$ by selling the fish! You can still get {rest}$ from market today'
          command_action:
            type: command
            value: 'money give {player} {money}'
      deny-icon:
        material: REDSTONE_BLOCK
        display:
          name: '<red><b>● <!b>Denied trade'
          lore:
            - '<font:uniform><gradient:#E6E6FA:red:#E6E6FA>Nothing to sell!</gradient></font>'
        action:
          sound_action:
            type: sound
            value:
              key: 'minecraft:entity.villager.no'
              source: 'player'
              volume: 1
              pitch: 1
      limit-icon:
        material: REDSTONE_BLOCK
        display:
          name: '<red><b>● <!b>Denied trade'
          lore:
            - '<font:uniform><gradient:#E6E6FA:red:#E6E6FA>The worth of items exceeds the money that can be earned for the rest of today!</gradient></font>'
        action:
          sound_action:
            type: sound
            value:
              key: 'minecraft:block.anvil.land'
              source: 'player'
              volume: 1
              pitch: 1

Copy

    decorative-icons:
      glass-pane:
        symbol: 'A'
        material: BLACK_STAINED_GLASS_PANE
        display:
          name: ' '

# 🏆 Loot | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

Loot configuration is closely integrated with item/block/entity configurations. This integration is vital to ensure that items/blocks/entities are properly registered as loot and can be invoked within the condition system.

**Unique Key Names for Loot:**

Every piece of loot should have a unique key name. No two loot items can have the same key name, preventing any potential conflicts.

**Integration with Other Configurations:**

For an item/block/entity to be registered as loot, it must be combined with its respective configuration. This ensures that the system recognizes the loot and its associated properties.

**Condition System Invocation:**

Once registered, the loot can be called upon within the condition system. This allows for more complex gameplay mechanics, such as spawning specific loot under certain conditions or scenarios.

**Nick:**

Determines what the loot shows like in fish finder and the return value of {nick} Every loot should have a nick, but most of the cases you don't have to manually set it. If a loot is item type, it would use "display.name" as nick if nick is not set, otherwise the nick would the loot ID.

*   **Example**:
    
    Copy
    
        nick: "<gold>This is a nick</gold>"
    

**Visibility in Fish Finder:**

Determines if the loot is visible or detectable when using a fish finder tool.

*   **Example**:
    
    Copy
    
        show-in-fishfinder: true
    

**Disable Statistics:**

If enabled, statistics related to this specific loot won't be tracked or displayed.

*   **Example**:
    

**Disable Global Event:**

If enabled, those events configurated in config.yml would no longer take effects on this loot

*   **Example**:
    

**Disable Mini-Games:**

Indicates if mini-games associated with this loot are disabled. Some items might be too worthless, making it preferable to skip the mini-game phase.

*   **Example**:
    

**Immediate Mini-Game Start:**

If set to true, upon encountering the loot, the related mini-game will commence immediately without any delay.

*   **Example**:
    

**Prevent grabbing:**

Prevent players from grabbing the dropped loots

*   **Example**:
    

**To inventory:**

Directly adds the loot to player's inventory

*   **Example**:
    

**Competition Score:**

Represents the score or value of the loot when used within competitions.

*   **Example**:
    

**Loot Group:**

The group of the loot, making it easier to modify the weight. If you don't know what weight is, read the article below

[⚖️ Weight System \[MUST READ\]chevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/weight-system-must-read)

*   **Example**:
    

**Statistics key:**

If you want different loots to share the same statistics you can add statistics key to the loot. For instance you have "tuna\_fish", "tuna\_fish\_silver\_star" and "tuna\_fish\_golden\_star", if you want %fishingstats\_size-record\_tuna% to return the max size of three, you can add this section to the three loots as follows:

**Base effects:**

Set the initial effects of the loot.

**Custom data: (since 2.2.20)**

Custom data allows you customize some special data for the loot and use it with internal placeholder `{data_xxx}` for instance `{data_max_weight}`. This allows you do many cool things for instance create weight properties to the item. Here's an example:

[Previous🧊 Blockchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/block)
[Next🗿 Totemchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/totem)

Last updated 11 months ago

Copy

    disable-stat: true

Copy

    disable-global-event: true

Copy

    disable-game: true

Copy

    instant-game: true

Copy

    prevent-grabbing: true

Copy

    to-inventory: true

Copy

    score: 10.5

Copy

    group: golden_star
    
    group:
      - golden_star
      - ocean

Copy

    statistics:
      # for amount of fish caught
      amount: tuna
      # for the best size record
      size: tuna

Copy

    base-effects:
      difficulty-adder: 10
      difficulty-multiplier: 0.9
      game-time-adder: 10
      game-time-multiplier: 0.9
      wait-time-adder: 10
      wait-time-multiplier: 0.9

Copy

    #contents/item/default.yml
    
    test:
      material: cod
      display:
        name: "A fish with weight!"
        lore:
          - "Weight: {data_weight}kg"
      nbt:
        Weight: "(Double) {data_weight}"
      price:
        base: 50
      custom-data:
        max_weight: 10
        min_weight: 5
        weight: "{weight}"
        some_text: "ABC"

Copy

    #config.yml
    
    placeholder-register:
      '{weight}': "%math_2:_{random}*({data_max_weight}-{data_min_weight})+{data_min_weight}%"
      
    # You can also use the data in price-formula and most places
    price-formula: "{base} + {size} * {bonus} + {data_weight} * 10"

# ✨ Effect | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect#introduction)

Introduction

Fishing effect is a temporary buff that gives players a boost for a single fishing attempt. This boost can come from fishing rods, bait, or even enchantments and totems! The fishing effect follows a specific configuration format. Below is how all the effects are set up.

All effects follow the format below:

Copy

    star_fishing_rod:
      requirements: # requirements for using this item
        ...
      effects: 
        effect_0: # effect name is customizable
          type: weight-mod
          # Aruguments
          value:
          - rubbish:-10
          - golden_star_fish:+10
          # Additional actions to run (Optional)
          actions:
            action_1:
              type: xxx
              value: xxx

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect#bait)

Bait


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use bait, it needs to be placed in offhand or fishing bag. Every time the rod is cast, it will be thrown together with the hook.

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect#hook)

Hook


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To equip hook on rod, make sure that you are in survival mode. Drag the hook onto your rod so it would be applied. To remove the hook from a rod, just right click the rod and the hook would be on your cursor.

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fi.imgur.com%2FA6RINzI.gif&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=63da7c12&sv=2)

hook and bait

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect#effect-library)

Effect Library


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> weight-mod (weight-mod offers a way to adjust the weight or chance of a single Loot, making it easier to quickly change the probability of obtaining a particular item. If there's no loot available, the effect would not take effect)

> weight-mod-ignore-conditions (The difference is that the effect would still take effect even if there's no such loot available)

> group-mod (Unlike weight-mod, group-mod allows you to modify the weight of multiple loots at the same time. Of course, an item can belong to multiple groups, like the 'gold quality' group and the 'marine' group. For guidance on how to assign loots to groups, refer to the Loot System)

> weight-group-ignore-conditions

> wait-time (Adjust the waiting time for a fish to bite on the hook)

> wait-time-multiplier (Adjust the waiting time for a fish to bite on the hook) ~(also named as "hook-time" in old versions)~

> difficulty (Adjust the game difficulty)

> difficulty-multiplier (Adjust the game difficulty)

> multiple-loot (Players can obtain multiple items in a single fishing attempt. Every 0.01 represents a 1% chance. If the value exceeds 1, players are guaranteed to get double the items with a small chance of getting triple. If the value surpasses 2, they are guaranteed to receive triple the items with a small chance of getting quadruple.)

> lava-fishing (Allow players to fish in lava)

> size (size offers a size boost for the loot, and the final size of the loot is added by this value. This option affects the scores in competitions where the fish size determines the points.)

> size-multiplier (size-bonus offers a size boost for the loot, and the final size of the loot is multiplied by this value. This option affects the scores in competitions where the fish size determines the points.)
> 
> ~(also named as "size-bonus" in old versions)~

> score (score gives a score boost during competitions, and the final score for the loot is added by this value. Note: This only works in TOTAL\_SCORE mode.)

> score-multiplier (score-bonus gives a score boost during competitions, and the final score for the loot is multiplied by this value. Note: This only works in TOTAL\_SCORE mode.) ~(also named as "score-bonus" in old versions)~

> game-time (game-time allows you to adjust the duration of the mini-game, giving players more time to react and more opportunities to succeed.)

> game-time-multiplier (game-time allows you to adjust the duration of the mini-game, giving players more time to react and more opportunities to succeed.)

> conditional (Apply condition system to some effects)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect#global-effects)

Global Effects

Global effects are located at config.yml. It allows you create global effects for players This is the default config which speeds up the fishing when there's a competition going on.

[Previous🛒 Marketchevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/market)
[Next🎉 Eventchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/event)

*   [Introduction](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect#introduction)
    
*   [Bait](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect#bait)
    
*   [Hook](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect#hook)
    
*   [Effect Library](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect#effect-library)
    
*   [Global Effects](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/effect#global-effects)
    

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: weight-mod
      value:
      - rubbish:-10
      - golden_star_fish:+10

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: weight-mod-ignore-conditions
      value:
      - enchantmentbook:+1

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: group-mod
      value:
      - gold:+20
      - normal:-6
    xxx_effect:
      type: group-mod
      value:
      - gold:+20
      - normal:-6

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: group-mod-ignore-conditions
      value:
      - enchantment:+10  

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: wait-time
      value: -20          <-  reduce the wait time by 20ticks

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: wait-time-multiplier
      value: 0.8          <-  ">1" make the time longer; "<1" the opposite
                          <-   -20% wait time

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: difficulty
      value: -17         <- -17 difficulty

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: difficulty-multiplier
      value: 0.7         <- -30% difficulty

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: multiple-loot
      value: 0.05

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: lava-fishing

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: size
      value: 10.5      <- +10.5 fish size

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: size-multiplier
      value: 1.3         <- +30% fish size

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: score
      value: 20         <- +20 score

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: score-multiplier
      value: 1.5        <- +50% score

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: game-time
      value: 10           <- +10 seconds

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: game-time-multiplier
      value: 1.3          <- +30% seconds

Copy

    xxx_effect:
      type: conditional
      conditions:
        ...
      effects:
        ...

Copy

    mechanics:
      global-effects:
        effect_1:
          type: conditional
          conditions:
            competition:
              ongoing: true
              id:
                - weekend_competition
          effects:
            effect_1:
              type: wait-time-multiplier
              value: 0.85

    delicate_hook:
      # Item part
      material: SHEARS
      display:
        name: '<#1E90FF>Delicate hook'
        lore:
          - ''
          - '<#7FFFD4>Desciption:'
          - '<gray> - An embodiment of craftsmanship and allure, the hook'
          - '<gray> - is not your average piece of tackle. Polished to'
          - '<gray> - perfection and intricately designed, it gleams in the'
          - '<gray> - water, irresistibly drawing high-quality fish closer.'
          - ''
          - '<#FFD700>Effects:'
          - '<gray> - Increase the chance of getting high quality fish'
      max-durability: 16  <- This property is required for a hook to work
      
      # Effect part
      effects:
        group:
          type: group-mod
          value:
            - silver_star:+1
            - golden_star:+1
     
      # Hook's unique property
      # Decides the lore on rod
      lore-on-rod:
        - ''
        - '<#7FFFAA>Equipped hook:'
        - '<gray> - Delicate hook: <white>{dur}<white> times left'

# 🐚 Command & Permission | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

The plugin's commands and corresponding permissions are completely customizable. You can modify it at will. The default commands and permission can be found on

[![Logo](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Ffluidicon.png&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd1317f9&sv=2)Custom-Fishing/core/src/main/resources/commands.yml at main · Xiao-MoMi/Custom-FishingGitHubchevron-right](https://github.com/Xiao-MoMi/Custom-Fishing/blob/main/core/src/main/resources/commands.yml)

commands.yml

The only permission which is hard coded is the permission node for the rows of fishing bag

Node

Description

fishingbag.rows.1~6

permission for fishing bag rows example: fishingbag.rows.2

[PreviousAuraSkillschevron-left](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/compatibility/auraskills)
[Next📊 Import & Export Datachevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/import-and-export-data)

# Supported levelers | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

mcMMO [https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/official-mcmmo-original-author-returns.64348/arrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/official-mcmmo-original-author-returns.64348/)

AureliumSkills AuraSkills [https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/aurelium-skills-advanced-skills-stats-abilities-and-more.81069/arrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/aurelium-skills-advanced-skills-stats-abilities-and-more.81069/)

JobsReborn [https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/jobs-reborn.4216/arrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/jobs-reborn.4216/)

EcoSkills [https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/ecoskills-%E2%AD%95-addictive-mmorpg-skills-%E2%9C%85-create-custom-skills-stats-effects-mana-%E2%9C%A8-plug-play.95541/arrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/ecoskills-%E2%AD%95-addictive-mmorpg-skills-%E2%9C%85-create-custom-skills-stats-effects-mana-%E2%9C%A8-plug-play.95541/)

EcoJobs [https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/ecojobs-%E2%AD%95-powerful-employment-system-%E2%9C%85-create-custom-jobs-%E2%9C%A8-levelling-effects.105190/arrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/ecojobs-%E2%AD%95-powerful-employment-system-%E2%9C%85-create-custom-jobs-%E2%9C%A8-levelling-effects.105190/)

MMOCore [https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/mmocore.70575/arrow-up-right](https://www.spigotmc.org/resources/mmocore.70575/)

Usage Example:

Copy

    tuna_fish:
      material: cod
      display:
        name: <gradient:#F0FFFF:#4682B4:#F0FFFF>Tuna Fish</gradient>
        lore:
          - <gray>Tuna is a kind of healthy food.
          - '<white>size: {size_formatted}cm'
      custom-model-data: 50001
      group:
        - ocean
        - no_star
      events:
        success:
          jobs_exp_action:
             type: plugin-exp
             value:
               plugin: JobsReborn
               exp: 15
               target: Fisherman

# ❓️ Common questions | CustomFishing | XiaoMoMi Plugins

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/common-questions#q1.-how-to-import-items-from-other-plugins)

Q1. How to import items from other plugins?

Hold the item in hand and run `/cfishing items import test_item`, you will find the exported item at `CustomFishing/imported_items.yml`, then you can copy and paste the exported data to the place you want.

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/common-questions#q2.-how-to-use-the-vanilla-1.20.5-custom-durability)

Q2. How to use the vanilla 1.20.5+ custom durability?

Firstly, delete the `max-durability` provided by the plugin so they would not conflict. Then use components section to add the `max_damage` property to the item. You can read this page for example

[🎁 Itemchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/item)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/common-questions#q3.-how-to-use-items-blocks-from-other-plugins)

Q3. How to use items/blocks from other plugins?

in config.yml there's a section like this, let's take items as example

Copy

    # CustomFishing supports using items/blocks from other plugins
    # If items share the same id, they would inherit the effects
    item-detection-order:
      - CustomFishing
      - vanilla
    block-detection-order:
      - vanilla

For instance if you have ItemsAdder installed, and you want CustomFishing to check ItemsAdder's ID, you can add ItemsAdder to the order:

Copy

    item-detection-order:
      - ItemsAdder
      - CustomFishing
      - vanilla

However, the items in ItemsAdder all have namespaces, so in order to ensure that the IDs correspond, you need to modify the fishing rod configuration of Custom Fishing

If you have MMOItems installed, you can configure like this (The capitalization used here is because MMOItems will convert all IDs to uppercase)

If you have Nexo installed, you can configure like this

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/common-questions#q4.-how-to-integrate-my-leveler-plugin-with-customfishing)

Q4. How to integrate my leveler plugin with CustomFishing?

Some leveler plugins may provide skill modification fishing mechanisms, and in this regard, Custom Fishing is powerless unless both developers work together. But in most cases, those attribute gains can be applied to Customs Fishing as long as the plugins provide corresponding attribute variables and skill level variables. You can refer to this page for some examples

[Supported levelerschevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/compatibility/supported-levelers)
[🅿️ Placeholder & Expressionchevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/placeholder-and-expression)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/common-questions#q5.-why-cant-i-have-minigames)

Q5. Why can't I have minigames?

If you have MMOCore installed, then your fishing mechanic would be like the picture below. The way to resolve the issue is deleting the fishing profession provided by MMOCore through deleting the YAML config.

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/common-questions#undefined)

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F4KsISSEnC2HEdscZY9PQ%2Fblobs%2FJb4zwMwy4K2rWnQPrs7s%2Fimage.png&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=33cab5ae&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/common-questions#q6.-how-to-enable-void-fishing-mechanic)

Q6. How to enable void-fishing mechanic?

Void fishing is a special mechanic registered by CustomFishing API. It allows registering any hook mechanic as you want if you know a little about coding. Firstly configure loots in loot-conditions.yml for the void for instance

Then create an effect that allows void-fishing at the place you want. In this case I'm using the `global-effects` in config.yml

Now you can fish in void!

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F4KsISSEnC2HEdscZY9PQ%2Fblobs%2FhunMQTaJ9kmFTQOvF16k%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e718da7&sv=2)

void fishing

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/common-questions#q7.-why-total_score-competition-not-works)

Q7. Why TOTAL\_SCORE competition not works?

You need to configure the score for each fish for this to work properly.

[🏆 Loot](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/format/loot)
 (See competition score on this page)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/common-questions#q8.-how-to-use-aureskills-mcmmo-fishing-loot-table)

Q8. How to use AureSkills/mcMMO fishing loot table

[mcMMO Treasurechevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/compatibility/mcmmo-treasure)
[AuraSkillschevron-right](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/compatibility/auraskills)

### 

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customfishing/plugin-wiki/customfishing/common-questions#q9.-how-to-fix-compatibility-issue-with-grappling-hook-plugins)

Q9. How to fix compatibility issue with grappling hook plugins

Take ExecuteableItems as an example, firstly add it to the `item-detection-order` in config.yml. Then add a rod blacklist requirement for it in config.yml

# ✅ Condition | CustomNameplates | XiaoMoMi Plugins

Plugin provides a powerful condition system. You can use both simple conditions and advanced conditions at the same time. Here are some examples for you to learn conditions.

Advanced condition allows you to use more conditions with the same type in one section

> simple biome condition

Copy

    biome:
      - minecraft:ocean
      - minecraft:deep_ocean
      - minecraft:cold_ocean
      - minecraft:deep_cold_ocean
      - minecraft:frozen_ocean
      - minecraft:deep_frozen_ocean
      - minecraft:lukewarm_ocean
      - minecraft:deep_lukewarm_ocean
      - minecraft:warm_ocean

> advanced condition (Allows you to use the same type of conditions) The section name ("requirement\_biome\_1" in this case) is completely customizable as long as it does not conflict with the condition type name.

Copy

    requirement_biome_1:
      type: biome
      refresh-interval: 5
      value:
        - minecraft:ocean
        - minecraft:deep_ocean
        - minecraft:cold_ocean
        - minecraft:deep_cold_ocean
        - minecraft:frozen_ocean
        - minecraft:deep_frozen_ocean
        - minecraft:lukewarm_ocean
        - minecraft:deep_lukewarm_ocean
        - minecraft:warm_ocean
    requirement_biome_2:
      type: '!biome'
      refresh-interval: 10 
      value:
        - minecraft:ocean
        - minecraft:deep_ocean
        - minecraft:cold_ocean

[hashtag](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/customnameplates/plugin-wiki/customnameplates/condition#condition-library)

Condition Library


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

> time (Minecraft game time 0~23999)

> ypos (Player's Y coordinate)

> biome (Supports custom biomes)

> world

> weather

> date (Real world date)

> permission

> “>” “>=” “<” “<=” “==” “!=”

> “startsWith” “endsWith” “equals” “contains” “in-list”

> logic (Create complex conditions)

> inverted (3.0.25+)

> level (Player exp level)

> random (0~1)

> cooldown

> regex

> environment

> potion-effect

> geyser/floodgate/is-bedrock-player (If the player is a badrock player)

> gamemode

> self-disguised (Requires LibsDisguises)

> disguised-type (Requires LibsDisguises)

> region (requires WorldGuard)

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FsgPn5qBKWdcU4vAzIOD2%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=935344cb&sv=2)

mode 1

![](https://mo-mi.gitbook.io/xiaomomi-plugins/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F38qW4kbjQZD9awFw00si%2Fblobs%2FS72ckLb0O9D9UgjMKeg9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb0990a0&sv=2)

mode 2

> is-passenger

> teammate (if two players are in the same team)

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    time:
      - 0~1000
      - 2000~6000
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: time
      value:
      - 0~1000
      - 2000~6000

Copy

    ypos:
      - 0~43
      - -45~12
      
    advanced_requirement:
      type: ypos
      value:
      - 0~43
      - -45~12

Copy

    biome:
      - minecraft:plains  <- whitelist
    
    '!biome':
      - minecraft:plains  <- blacklist
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: biome
      value:
      - minecraft:plains
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: '!biome'
      value:
      - minecraft:plains

Copy

    world:
      - world
    
    '!world':
      - blacklist_world
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: world
      value:
      - world
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: '!world'
      value:
      - blacklist_world

Copy

    weather:
      - thunder
      - rainstorm
      - clear
      - rain
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'weather'
      value:
      - thunder
      - clear
      - rain

Copy

    date:
      - 12/25
      - 6/1
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'date'
      value:
      - 12/25
      - 6/1

Copy

    permission: customfishing.admin
    
    '!permission': blacklist.perm
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'permission'
      value: customfishing.admin
      
    advanced_requirement:
      type: '!permission'
      value: blacklist.perm

Copy

    '==':
      value1: '20'
      value2: '%player_health%'
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: '=='
      value:
        value1: '20'
        value2: '%player_health%'

Copy

    '!startsWith':
      value1: '%player_name%'
      value2: 'X'  <- player names that are not starting with "X"
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'contains'
      value:
        value1: '%player_name%'
        value2: '_'  <- player names that contain "_"
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: '!equals'
      value:
        value1: '%player_name%'
        value2: 'XiaoMoMi'  <- player names that not equal "XiaoMoMi"
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'in-list'
      value:
        papi: '%player_name%'
        values: 
          - 'XiaoMoMi'
          - 'XIAOMOMI'
          - 'XlA0M0Ml'

Copy

    advanced_requirement:
      type: '&&'
      value:
        in-lava: true
        requirement_time:
          type: time
          value:
            - 0~12000
        '||':
          world:
            - world_nether
          '&&':
            ypos:
              - -64~-32
            world:
              - world

Copy

    inverted:
      requireent_1:
        type: "||"
        value:
           world:
            - world_nether
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'inverted'
      value:
        requirement_world:
          type: world
          value:
            - world_nether

Copy

    level: 10
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'level'
      value: 10

Copy

    random: 0.3   <- 30% chance
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'random'
      value: 0.7   <- 70% chance

Copy

    cooldown:
      key: unique
      time: 1000 #ms
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'cooldown'
      value:
        key: A
        time: 100 #ms

Copy

    regex:
      papi: "%xxx%"
      regex: "[A-Z]"
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'regex'
      value:
        papi: "%xxx%"
        regex: "[A-Z]"

Copy

    environment:
      - normal
      - nether
      - the_end
      
    advanced_requirement:
      type: '!environment'
      value:
        - nether
        - the_end
        - custom

Copy

    potion-effect: "LUCK>=0"
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'potion-effect'
      value: "LUCK!=-1"
    
    "-1": Player doesn't have such a potion effect
    "value no lower than 0": The potion effect's amplifier
    
    Examples:
      LUCK==1
      LUCK<5
      LUCK>=0

Copy

    geyser: false
    floodgate: false
      
    advanced_requirement:
      type: 'geyser'
      value: true
    
    is-bedrock-player: true

Copy

    gamemode:
      - survival
    
    advanced_requirement:
      type: "!gamemode"
      value:
      - adventure

Copy

    self-disguised: false

Copy

    '!disguised-type':
      - ARROW

Copy

    advanced_requirement:
      type: region
      value:
        mode: 1 # 1,2
        values:
          - a
          - b
    region:
      mode: 2
      values:
        - a
        - b

Copy

    'is-passenger': true

Copy

    teammate: true
